Noteholders, will be carried out through: 
1.- The regular ordinary notices referred in paragraph III.5.3 a), by means of their 
publication in the AIAF daily bulletin or any other that substitutes it in the future 
or of similar characteristics, or by means of their publication in a newspaper of 
wide distribution in Spain, be it economic-financial or a general newspaper. 
2.- The extraordinary notices referred in paragraph III.5.3 b) 1. above, except that 
in connection with the Nominal Interest Rates of all Classes of Notes determined 
for the first Interest Accrual Period and the final spreads applicable to each Class 
of Notes, and, where appropriate, the notice on Barclays Bank, S.A. finally acting 
as Underwriting Entity, by means of their publication in the daily gazzette of 
AIAF, and those referred to in paragraph III.5.3. b) 2 above, by means of their 
publication in a newspaper of wide distribution in Spain, whether of an economic-
financial or a general nature. 
Additionally, the previous notifications may be served by means of their publication in 
other means of general diffusion.   
Additionally, the previous notifications may be served by means of their publication in 
the web page of the Managing Company (www.ahorroytitulizacion.com).   
 
 
97 


 
For these purposes, the notifications will be considered as served in the date of their 
publication, being appropriate for such publication any day of the calendar, whether  
or not a Business Day. 
d) Information to be furnished to CNMV and the Rating Agencies 
The Managing Company, in representing the Fund, will inform the CNMV and the 
Rating Agencies of any publication whether of a regular or of an extraordinary nature 
which may be carried out as provided above, as well as any information which may be 
requested from such company, notwithstanding what is said above. 
III.6. 
Tax Regime of the Fund 
Article 7.1.g) of Royal Legislative Decree 4/2004, of March 5, on Corporate Tax 
provides that Funds of this nature are subject to the general Corporate Income Tax 
rate (currently, 35%).  
The management and the deposit and management services rendered to the Fund by 
the Managing Company are exempt from Value Added Tax, in accordance with Law 
19/1992 and Article 20.1.18 of Law 37/1992, of December 28, on Value Added Tax.   
The incorporation of the Fund will be exempt from Capital Tax, as provided by the 
Transfer Tax Law and Law 19/1992. 
The issue, reimbursement and repayment of the Notes are exempt from Value Added 
Tax (section 20.1 no. 18 of the Value Added Tax Law) and from Transfer Tax and 
Stamp Duty (section 45-I.B no. 15 of Legislative Royal Decree 1/1993 of September 
24 which approves the Transfer Tax and Stamp Duty Law).  
The returns on the Mortgage Shares, loans or other rights of credit which constitute 
income for the Fund shall not be subject to withholding tax nor to payment on 
account (section 59, paragraph k) of Royal-Decree 1777/2004, on Corporate Income 
Tax Regulations). 
Finally, the subscription of the Mortgage Shares by the Fund is exempt from Value 
Added Tax (Article 20.1 no. 18 of Law 37/1992 on Value Added Tax).  
III.7. 
Exceptional amendment events of the Incorporation Deed of the Fund 
The Incorporation Deed will essentially include the following contents: (i) identification 
of the Mortgage Shares; (ii) precise definition of the content of the Notes to be 
issued; and (iii) determination of the transactions that the Managing Company, in the 
name of the Fund, is entitled to carry out, for the purposes of increasing security or 
regularity in the payment of the Notes and covering the temporary delays between 
the calendar of the flows of principal and interest of the Mortgage Shares and that of 
the Notes. In this regard, the Incorporation Deed shall establish that the Fund, 
through its Managing Company, will enter into the agreements set out in paragraphs 
V.3 and V.4. 
 
 
98 


 
In accordance with Article 5.3 of Law 19/1992 none of the Incorporation Deed of the 
Fund, the issue and subscription of Mortgage Shares and the issue of the Notes may 
be altered except in the extraordinary events and in accordance with the conditions 
established by the applicable regulations, although it may be amended at the request 
of the CNMV, provided that the ratings of the Notes and the interests of the holders of 
the Notes are not adversely affected. Additionally, the Incorporation Deed will not be 
registered with the Mercantile Registry. 
III.8. 
Liquidation of the Fund 
III.8.1. Early liquidation of the Fund 
The Managing Company, in all those events of early repayment included in paragraph 
II.11.3.3, once the Fund is liquidated and within a maximum term of six (6) months 
since the distribution of the Fund assets referred to in such paragraph, in accordance 
with the payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the Fund provided in 
paragraph V.6.1 and the exceptional rules provided in paragraph V.6.2, will execute a 
notarial deed to be sent to the CNMV, in which the following information shall be 
provided: 
(i) 
the reasons, set out in the Incorporation Deed and in the Prospectus, that gave 
rise to the liquidation of the Fund; 
(ii) the communication procedure to the Noteholders and the CNMV of the 
anticipated repayment of the Notes; and 
(iii) the distribution of the available funds of the Fund following the payment priority 
order in the event of liquidation of the Fund set out in paragraph V.6.1 and the 
exceptional rules provided in paragraph V.6.2. 
The necessary requirements for the anticipated liquidation of the Fund are the 
following: 
(i) 
That the payment obligations derived from the Notes issued by the Fund can be 
satisfied and cancelled in their entirety (in the event the Managing Company 
decides to early liquidate the Fund if the outstanding balance is less than 10% of 
the initial balance of the Mortgage Shares portfolio) or, otherwise, that the 
Managing Company, before proceeding to the anticipated liquidation of the Fund, 
calls the Noteholders, for information purposes exclusively. 
The payment obligations derived from the Notes on the date of early liquidation of 
the Fund are the Unpaid Principal Balance on that date plus the accrued and 
unpaid interest until the early repayment date, reduced, as the case may be, by 
the relevant withholding tax; all these amounts will be considered on that date and 
to all legal effects, as due and payable. 
 
 
99 


 
(ii) That the resolution of early liquidation of the Fund adopted by the Managing 
Company is communicated to the Noteholders, in the form set out in paragraph 
III.5.3 and with thirty (30) Business Days’ advanced notice, 
This communication, which must have been previously served to the CNMV, will 
contain the description of (i) the events giving rise to the anticipated liquidation 
of the Fund, (ii) the procedure to carry out the liquidation, described in the 
following paragraph, and (iii) the way to satisfy and cancel the payment 
obligations derived from the Notes. 
In order to carry out the anticipated liquidation of the Fund and the anticipated 
repayment of the Note issue in the events and with the requirements indicated in this 
paragraph and, as the case may be, in order for the Fund to have enough liquidity to 
pay the Unpaid Principal Balance of the Notes and the accrued and unpaid interest 
until the early repayment, the Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the 
Fund: 
(i) 
shall sell the Mortgage Shares at a price not lower than the market price. For 
these purposes, the Managing Company shall request offers from, at least, five 
(5) of the most active entities in the trading of mortgage backed financial 
instruments in the local markets, and shall not be allowed to sell the Mortgage 
Shares at a price lower than the best of the offers received. The Issuer will have 
a preemptive right to acquire the whole (but not part) of said Mortgage Shares in 
the conditions determined by the Managing Entity and, in any event, for a price 
equal or higher than the best of the offers received from the above referred 
entities. As from the date the Managing Company notifies the conditions under 
which it would be prepared to sell the relevant Mortgage Shares, the Issuer will 
have ten (10) Business Days to exercise the preemptive right. This right shall 
under no circumstance be considered as a repurchase commitment or 
undertaking on the side of the Issuer; 
(ii) will cancel the agreements that are not necessary for the liquidation process of 
the Fund; 
(iii) finally, if the previous actions prove insufficient or if there are assets remaining, it 
shall sell the assets which belong to the Fund. The Managing Company will be 
authorised to accept those offers that, in its opinion, cover the market value of 
the relevant asset and be paid in cash. Exceptionally, it will be entitled to accept 
payment delays for a term not greater than two (2) years. To establish the 
market value, the Managing Company may be entitled to obtain the reports that 
it may find appropriate. The Issuer will have a pre-emptive right, in such a way 
that it may acquire the said assets that belong to the Fund before any third 
party. The Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, shall 
send to the Issuer a list of the assets and offers received from third parties, and 
the Issuer will be able to make use of the aforementioned right regarding all the 
assets offered by the Managing Company within the thirty (30) days following the 
 
 
100 


 
receipt of the communication and whenever its offers are equivalent, at least, to 
the best third party offer. 
The Managing Company, once the reserve referred in paragraph III.8.2 has been 
accounted for, shall allocate all the amounts obtained from the transfer of assets 
which belong to the Fund to the payment of the different items, in the manner, 
amount and preference payment order in the event of liquidation of the Fund 
established in paragraph V.6.1. and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph V.6.2. 
III.8.2. Extinguishment of the Fund 
The Fund will be extinguished, due to either the entire repayment of the Mortgage 
Shares that it owns, or the early liquidation procedure provided in paragraph III.8.1 
above, in the even that any of the extinguishment events included in the Prospectus 
(which are listed below, without limitation) or provided by Law occurs: 
(i) 
in the case of entire repayment of the Mortgage Shares (paragraph II.11.3.3); 
(ii) in the event of failure of any of the Rating Agencies to confirm the provisional 
ratings of the Notes prior to the commencement of the Subscription Period 
(paragraph II.3); 
(iii) when the Managing Company decides the early liquidation of the Fund if the 
Principal Balance of the Mortgage Shares is less than 10% of the initial balance of 
the Mortgage Shares portfolio provided that the early repayment of the Mortgage 
Shares plus the existing balance of the Cash Account and, as the case may be, of 
the Excess Balance Account, allows a total cancellation of the obligations due to 
the Noteholders, after fulfilling the payment priority order as described in 
paragraph V.6.1. and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph V.6.2. 
(paragraph II.11.3.3); 
(iv) if by reason of any event or exceptional circumstance not expected on the 
Incorporation Date, the financial balance of the Fund required by Law 19/1992 is 
permanently and negatively affected for reasons not attributable to the operation 
of the Fund, such as a new legal regime or additional legal regulations, 
withholdings or other situations that could affect this balance permanently 
(paragraph II.11.3.3); 
(v) in the event that a relevant breach of payment exists or it is foreseen that there 
will be one, and such breach produces a significant permanent unbalance related 
to any of the Notes issued (paragraph II.11.3.3); 
(vi)  in the case of full repayment of the Notes (no later than the Final Maturity Date) 
(paragraph II.11.3.3); 
(vii) in the event of early liquidation of the Fund and repayment of the Notes if the 
Managing Company is declared to be in liquidation or insolvency (“concurso”), or 
 
 
101 


 
in case its authorisation has been revoked and a new Managing Company has not 
been designated within a term of four months in accordance with paragraph 
III.3.1 (paragraph II.11.3.3). 
If during the liquidation of the Fund and once all the payments have been made by 
means of the distribution of the available funds according to the payment priority 
order in the event of liquidation of the Fund settled down in paragraph V.6.1. and the 
exceptional rules set out in  paragraph V.6.2, there are any amounts remaining, they 
shall be paid to the Issuer. In the event that the remaining amount was not liquid 
because the assets are Mortgage Shares pending judicial or notarial resolution in 
proceedings initiated as a consequence of the default of the debtor in the payment of 
the Participated Mortgage Loan, in accordance with paragraph IV.2.11, both its 
continuance, and the result of the court decision will be in favour of the Issuer. 
The Managing Company will not extinguish the Fund and cancel its registration with 
the corresponding administrative registries until the remaining assets of the Fund are 
liquidated and the Available Funds are distributed, following the payment priority 
order in the event of liquidation of the Fund of paragraph V.6.1. and the exceptional 
rules set out in paragraph V.6.2, except for the appropriate reserve to pay the final 
extinguishment expenses. 
Six (6) months after the liquidation of the remaining assets of the Fund and the 
distribution of the Available Funds, the Managing Company will execute a notarial 
deed that will be sent to the CNMV and the Rating Agencies, declaring: (i) the 
extinguishment of the Fund and the reasons that gave rise to it; (ii) the procedure 
used to inform the Noteholders and the CNMV; and (iii) the distribution of the 
Available Funds following the payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the 
Fund established in paragraph V.6.1. and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph 
V.6.2. The Managing Company will publish said statements in a newspaper of national 
distribution in compliance with the remaining applicable administrative steps.

IV.1. 
Description of the Mortgage Shares that are grouped in the Fund 
The Issuer is the holder of the Participated Mortgage Loans described in this Chapter. 
The Issuer shall issue the Mortgage Shares in accordance with Law 2/1981, of March 
25, Royal Decree 685/1982, of March 17 as amended by Royal Decree 1289/1991, of 
August 2, so that the Managing Company groups them in the Fund in accordance with 
Law 19/1992 and other applicable regulations. Given the corporate investor nature of 
the Fund, the issue of the Mortgage Shares will not be recorded with a marginal note 
in each recording of the mortgages with the Land Registry. 
The total face value of the Mortgage Shares issue will be at least equal to the initial 
total nominal amount of the Notes issued. Each Mortgage Share represents 100% of 
the principal and of the interest pending amortisation and payment, respectively, as 
well as of the arrears interest of each one of the Participated Mortgage Loans to which 
it corresponds, all in accordance with paragraph IV.1.c). 
The Participated Mortgage Loans are part of a selection of mortgage loans whose 
characteristics are indicated in paragraph IV.4. The principal balance of the selected 
Participated Mortgage Loans at May 16, 2005, amounted to 709,644,270.35 euros. 
This amount will be adjusted on the Incorporation Date as much as possible to the 
amount of the issue of Notes, that is, 700,000,000 euros. 
a) 
Identification of the Credit Entity issuing such shares   
There is only one entity issuing the Mortgage Shares, namely, Barclays Bank, S.A., 
holder of the underlying Participated Mortgage Loans. 
 
Representations of the Issuer 
The Issuer, as holder of the Participated Mortgage Loans until the Mortgage Shares 
issue, represents and warrants to the Managing Company, on behalf of the Fund: 
(1) that it is a duly incorporated credit entity in accordance with the applicable 
legislation, registered with the Mercantile Registry and authorized to participate 
in the mortgage market; 
(2) that, neither on the date of registration of the present Prospectus, nor at any 
time from its incorporation has it been in a situation of insolvency (“concurso”); 
 
 
103 


 
(3) that the Mortgage Shares shall be issued in accordance with Law 19/1992, of July 
7, Law 2/1981, Royal Decree 685/1982, Royal Decree 1289/1991, and other 
applicable regulations, shall comply with all the requirements established therein, 
and shall be suitable to be grouped in a Mortgage Securitisation Fund; 
(4) that its corporate bodies have validly adopted all the necessary resolutions for 
the issue of the Mortgage Shares and to execute the Incorporation Deed, the 
agreements and the complementary undertakings assumed therein;   
(5) that the Participated Mortgage Loans exist and are valid and enforceable in 
accordance with the applicable legislation;   
(6) that it is holder of all the Participated Mortgage Loans and of the associated real 
estate mortgages, there being no impediment for the issue of the Mortgage 
Shares; 
(7) that the data regarding the Participated Mortgage Loans, which are included in 
this Prospectus and will be included in the Incorporation Deed, are complete and 
provide a true and exact representation of the Participated Mortgage Loans;   
(8) that all the Participated Mortgage Loans are guaranteed by real estate mortgage 
incorporated as first in rank over the complete domain of each and every one of 
the relevant properties, and the mortgaged properties are not affected by 
transfer limitations, conditions subsequent or any other domain limitation; 
(9) that all the Participated Mortgage Loans are formalized in notarial deed and all 
the mortgages have been correctly constituted and recorded with the relevant 
Land Registries and that the registration of the mortgaged properties is in force 
and without any contradiction and is not subject to any effective limitation 
preceding the mortgage in rank, in accordance with the applicable regulations;   
(10) that all mortgagors are individuals resident in Spain; 
(11) that the Participated Mortgage Loans have been granted to finance individuals in 
the construction, acquisition or renovation of residential properties or 
subrogations to individuals of financings to promoters for dwellings for sale or 
lease; 
(12) that the mortgages are constituted over properties that belong to the relevant 
mortgagor in fee simple, the Issuer being unaware of any litigation existing 
regarding the ownership of these properties which may damage the mortgages; 
(13) that the mortgaged properties have been appraised by entities appropriately 
authorised for this purpose, the said entities are validly registered with the 
relevant Official Registries of the Bank of Spain, the appraisal being evidenced by 
means of the appropriate certification and that the appraisals carried out comply 
with all the requirements established in the legislation on the mortgage market;   
 
 
104 


 
(14) that the principal balance of each of the Participated Mortgage Loans does not 
exceed 80% of the appraisal value of the properties mortgaged as guarantee of 
the corresponding Participated Mortgage Loan; 
(15) that it is unaware of any reduction in the value of any property mortgaged in 
more than 20% of the appraisal value;   
(16) that the residential properties over which the mortgage guarantee has been 
constituted have an insurance policy against damages in force, by means of 
which the capital insured is not lower than their appraisal value, excluding the 
non-insurable parts, Barclays Bank, S.A. has signed an agreement with an 
insurance entity for a global policy of subsidiary insurance that covers the scope 
of the damages insurance in the event that it does not exist or the insured capital 
is insufficient, for the Participated Mortgage Loans, for the total amount of the 
Note issue; 
(17) that the Participated Mortgage Loans are not represented in titles, whether 
registered or bearer titles; 
(18) that, on the Incorporation Date, none of the Participated Mortgage Loans will 
have unpaid matured debts for a term exceeding thirty (30) days;   
(19) that it does not have knowledge that any of the debtors of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans is holder of any credit right against the Issuer that confers them 
the right to set-off; 
(20) that the information contained in this Prospectus and regarding the issue of 
Notes from the Participated Mortgage Loans portfolio and from the Mortgage 
Shares is accurate and complete; 
(21) that the granting of the Participated Mortgage Loans and the Mortgage Shares 
issue, as well as all acts related to them, have been carried out or will be carried 
out according to the market criteria; 
(22) that the criteria established by the Issuer in the Memorandum on Loan Granting 
Criteria that will be attached to the Incorporation Deed as an Annex, have been 
fully complied with in the granting of all Participated Mortgage Loans;   
(23) that all mortgage deeds constituted over the properties to which the Participated 
Mortgage Loans refer are correctly deposited in the files of the Issuer prepared 
for this purpose in favour of the Managing Company and all Participated 
Mortgage Loans are clearly identified, in electronic means and in their deeds; 
(24) that, on the Incorporation Date, the total principal balance of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans shall be equal to the total sum of the initial capital amounts of all 
the Mortgage Shares to be issued, and which shall at least be equal to the initial 
total nominal amount of the Notes;   
 
 
105 


 
(25) that from the date of their granting, the Participated Mortgage Loans have been 
and are being managed by the Issuer in accordance with the usual procedures of 
the Issuer; 
(26) that it does not have knowledge of any litigation related to the Participated 
Mortgage Loans which may affect their validity or which may result in the 
application of article 1,535 of the Spanish Civil Code, or of the existence of 
circumstances which may result in the mortgage deed granted as security for the 
Participated Mortgage Loans being ineffective; 
(27) that, as far as it is concerned, the accrued premiums until the issue date for the 
insurance policies subscribed, which relate to paragraph (16) above, have been 
entirely satisfied;   
(28) that all Participated Mortgage Loans have a final maturity date not exceeding 
October 29, 2034;   
(29) that all the Participated Mortgage Loans have a maximum of 12 instalments per 
year;   
(30) that, on the date of registration of the Prospectus, the Issuer has not received 
any notification of total early repayment of the Participated Mortgage Loans; 
(31) that it is unaware of any circumstance that prevents the enforcement of the 
mortgage guarantee;   
(32) that the Participated Mortgage Loans are not linked to any issue of mortgage 
notes or Mortgage Shares, other than the Mortgage Shares issue;  
(33) that, once the Mortgage Shares are issued, the volume of mortgage debentures 
(cédulas hipotecarias) issued by the Issuer and pending maturity shall not exceed 
90% of the sum of the non-amortised capital of the mortgage loans in portfolio 
appropriate for covering the issue, in accordance with Articles 59 and 60 of Royal 
Decree 685/1982, amended by Royal Decree 1289/1991; 
(34) that all mortgaged properties as security for the Participated Mortgage Loans are 
located in Spain; 
(35) that the mortgaged properties as security for the Participated Mortgage Loans 
are not ineligible as assets excluded for standing as security under article 31.1 of 
Royal Decree 685/1982, nor do the Participated Mortgage Loans have any of the 
credit features excluded or restricted under article 32 of Royal Decree 685/1982; 
and 
(36) that the Mortgage Shares will be issued with the same maturity and interest rate 
than the underlying Participated Mortgage Loans and for an amount equivalent to 
 
 
106 


 
the principal balance of the Participated Mortgage Loans on the Incorporation 
Date.   
The Issuer undertakes to provide to the Managing Company, all periodic 
information about the Mortgage Shares, in accordance with the electronic means 
available to the Managing Company. 
b) 
Number and amount of Mortgage Shares grouped in the Fund 
The Mortgage Shares that will be issued for their subscription by the Fund on the 
Incorporation Date will have a total capital value at least equal to the total nominal 
amount of the Notes, that is, Euro 700,000,000.   
The issue price of the Mortgage Shares will be the par value. The price that the Fund 
shall pay for the subscription of the Mortgage Shares will be equal, therefore, to the 
sum of the nominal amount of each Mortgage Share. 
The payment of the issue price of the Mortgage Shares will be made on the 
Disbursement Date of the Notes (referred in paragraph II.18.5) together with the 
accrued interest at the reference interest rate applicable to the first Interest Accrual 
Period between the date of granting of the Incorporation Deed (included) and the 
Disbursement Date (excluded). 
Additionally, the Issuer will be entitled to receive an amount equal to the ordinary 
interest accrued by the Participated Mortgage Loans from the last date of settlement 
of interest of each one of them until the Incorporation Date and to the arrears interest 
which the Participated Mortgage Loans may have accrued from the relevant non-
payment date until the Incorporation Date (the “Accrued Interest”) that will be 
paid, as the case may be, as and when they are received by the Fund. 
c) 
Rights of Mortgage Share holders over the loans that guarantee said 
Mortgage Shares 
The Mortgage Shares refer to a participation of 100% in the principal and in the 
interest, (including ordinary and arrears interest), of each Participated Mortgage Loan. 
The Issuer, in accordance with Article 5.8 of Law 19/1992, is not subject to the risk of 
default in payment of the Mortgage Shares and, therefore, does not assume any 
liability for the default of the mortgagors, either of principal, of interest or of any 
other amount that they could owe by virtue of the Participated Mortgage Loans. The 
participation in the Participated Mortgage Loans will be for the remaining term until 
the final maturity of the Participated Mortgage Loans. The Issuer will assume no 
responsibility in warranting directly or indirectly the appropriate completion of the 
transaction, neither shall it grant guarantees or backings, or enter into repurchasing 
agreements of the Mortgage Shares, except as provided in paragraph IV.1.d) and 
IV.1.e). 
 
 
107 


 
The Mortgage Shares confer the following rights in relation to the Participated 
Mortgage Loans: 
a) 
to receive all amounts accrued for the repayment of the principal of the 
Participated Mortgage Loans; 
b) 
to receive all amounts accrued for the ordinary interest of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans; 
c) 
to receive all amounts accrued for arrears interest of the Participated Mortgage 
Loans; 
d) 
to receive any other amounts, assets or rights in payment of principal, interest or 
expenses of the Participated Mortgage Loans, both for the auction price or the 
amount determined by a judicial decision or notarial procedure when enforcing 
the mortgage guarantees, for the transfer or operation of the assigned properties 
or as a consequence of the mentioned enforcements, in management and interim 
possession of the properties in an enforcement procedure; and 
e) 
to receive all possible rights or compensation that may arise in favour of the 
Issuer, including, not only those deriving from the insurance policies related to 
the loans, which are also assigned by the Issuer to the Fund, but also those 
deriving from any accessory right to the Participated Mortgage Loan, and 
excluding the fees established in each one of the Participated Mortgage Loans, 
which will remain for the account of the Issuer as part of the price in accordance 
with paragraph IV.1.b). 
All the aforementioned rights will accrue in favour of the Fund from the date of 
granting of the Incorporation Deed and issue of the Mortgage Shares, except for the 
ordinary interest and the arrears interest, which will accrue from the last interest 
liquidation date of each of the Participated Mortgage Loans and from the non-
payment date, as the case may be, of the relevant Participated Mortgage Loans, 
respectively, both dates being prior to or equal to the Incorporation Date. This 
notwithstanding, an amount equal to the ordinary interest accrued from the last 
coupon payment date to the Incorporation Date and to the arrears interest which the 
Participated Mortgage Loans may have accrued from the relevant non-payment date 
to the Incorporation Date shall be paid to the Issuer in accordance with paragraph 
IV.1.b).  
The rights of the Fund resulting from the Mortgage Shares are tied to the payments 
made by the debtors of the Participated Mortgage Loans and, therefore, they are 
directly affected by the evolution, delays, cash advances or any other issue affecting 
them. 
Until the granting of the Incorporation Deed, the Issuer will be beneficiary of the 
insurance policies against damages subscribed by the mortgagors with regard to the 
 
 
108 


 
mortgaged properties, in guarantee of the Participated Mortgage Loans, up to the 
secured amount, with each one of the Participated Mortgage Loan deeds authorising 
that, in the event of default of payment of the corresponding insurance premium by 
the debtor (policyholder), the Issuer, as mortgage creditor, may satisfy at the expense 
of the debtor, the amount that corresponds to the premium. By means of the 
Incorporation Deed of the Fund, the Issuer will formalise the assignment of the rights 
corresponding to it as beneficiary of these insurance policies against damages 
subscribed by the mortgagors or any other insurance policy which may grant an 
equivalent cover. All the amounts that should be collected by the Issuer regarding this 
item shall be accrued due, therefore, to the Fund, as holder of the Mortgage Shares. 
The payments made to the Fund as interest of the Mortgage Shares will not be 
subject to withholding as established in Article 59.k) of Royal Decree 1777/2004, of 
July 30, by means of which the Corporate Tax Regulation is approved. 
d) 
Rules foreseen for the substitution of Mortgage Shares in the event of early 
repayment of those initially contained in the Fund 
In the event of early repayment of the Mortgage Shares following the anticipated 
reimbursement of the principal of the Participated Mortgage Loans, the substitution of 
the affected Mortgage Shares will not be carried out. 
If, while the Mortgage Shares are in force, it is detected that any of them did not 
conform on the Incorporation Date to the conditions and characteristics described in 
paragraph IV.1.a), the Issuer undertakes, subject to the Managing Company’s 
consent, to immediately substitute or, as the case may be, repay the relevant 
Mortgage Share, subject to the following rules: 
1. 
The substitution by the Issuer, which, in any event, shall be carried out at a value 
equivalent to the face value (capital outstanding and capital due but not paid to 
the Fund, on each of the Mortgage Shares) plus accrued and unpaid interest, shall 
be performed by issuing Mortgage Shares from loans of its portfolio which may be 
grouped together in a Mortgage Securitisation Fund, provided that such new loan 
bears characteristics which are homogeneous to those of the underlying 
Participated Mortgage Loan of the replaced Mortgage Share in relation to its 
amount, term (not exceeding the deadline for maturity of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans), interest rate, characteristics of the debtor or characteristics of 
the mortgaged property, as well as credit quality in terms of the relationship 
between the Principal Balance of the Mortgage Share and the appraisal value of 
the property which is the subject of the guarantee of the underlying loan. 
Should there be no loans in the Issuer portfolio of similar characteristics to the 
Participated Mortgage Loan underlying the substituted Mortgage Share within the 
term of 15 calendar days as from the communication referred to in paragraph 2.1 
below, the Issuer undertakes to repay the affected Mortgage Shares, immediately 
reimbursing in cash the pending capital, the accrued and unpaid interest, as well 
 
 
109 


 
as any amount that may be accrued due to the Fund until that date as provided in 
the corresponding Mortgage Share. 
2. 
The substitution will be carried out in the following way: 
2.1. The Issuer shall communicate to the Managing Company the existence of the 
affected or unsuitable Mortgage Share and the Managing Company will provide its 
prior consent to the replacement (as described in paragraph II.15). Subsequently, 
the Issuer will immediately cancel this Mortgage Share and will issue another 
Mortgage Share of similar characteristics of residual term, interest rate, pending 
principal value and credit quality in terms of the relationship existing between the 
pending principal of the Mortgage Share and the appraisal value of the property 
which is the object of the guarantee of the underlying Participated Mortgage Loan. 
Prior to the substitution, a confirmation of the suitability of the loan substituting 
the former must been given by an external auditing firm, in accordance with 
paragraph I.3, that the financial structure of the Fund is not affected by the 
substitution. 
2.2. The issue of the Mortgage Share by the Issuer and the substitution by the 
Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, will be made by 
means of the execution of a notarial deed including the data related to the 
Mortgage Share that should be substituted and to its underlying Participated 
Mortgage Loan, and the data related to the newly issued Mortgage Share, with the 
data of the Participated Mortgage Loan, as well as the reason for the substitution 
and the variables that determine the homogeneous nature of both Mortgage 
Shares, according to that described previously. Such deed shall be executed within 
the term of 30 calendar days as from the communication referred to in paragraph 
2.1 above. A copy of this deed shall be sent to the CNMV, to the Sociedad de 
Gestión de los Sistemas de Registro, Compensación y Liquidación de Valores, S.A. 
and to AIAF and it shall be communicated to the Rating Agencies. Furthermore, 
the Managing Company will deliver to the Issuer the multiple share certificate and 
the Issuer will issue a new multiple title representing the Mortgage Shares 
(excluding the substituted Mortgage Share and including the new Mortgage Share). 
e) 
Other conditions established in the issue of said Mortgage Shares and in the 
subscription by the Fund and the applicable provisions, as the case may be, 
for the transfer of the Mortgage Shares 
The Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, will fully subscribe 
the Mortgage Shares issued by the Issuer in the same act as the Fund is incorporated 
and the Incorporation Deed is granted. The total price that the Fund, acting through 
the Managing Company, will pay for the subscription of the Mortgage Shares will be 
the nominal amount of the issued Mortgage Shares, plus the interest corresponding to 
the payment deferral of such nominal amount from the Incorporation Date to the 
Disbursement Date. The price that the Managing Company, in the name and on behalf 
of the Fund, will pay to the Issuer will be paid before 17:00 hours of the same 
 
 
110 


 
Business Day when the Notes issue is entirely disbursed according to paragraph 
II.18.5. 
The subscriber is the Fund AyT Génova Hipotecario VI, FTH which is subject to Law 
19/1992. The Fund will constitute a separate and closed estate, without a separate 
and independent legal status. As regard its assets, by the Mortgage Shares and the 
Reserve Fund referred to in paragraph V.3.4 and, as for its liabilities, by the Notes and 
the Subordinated Loans described in paragraphs V.3.2 and V.3.3, in such a way that 
the net value of the Fund will be zero. 
The Mortgage Shares and the Notes to be issued will be described in the 
Incorporation Deed. The Incorporation Deed may not be amended (except in 
exceptional circumstances, and under the conditions that will be described in future 
regulation developments of Law 19/1992) and, therefore, no additional issues of 
securities may be carried out. 
As established in the Royal Decree 685/1982 of the Mortgage Market Regulation, 
modified by Royal Decree 1289/91, the Mortgage Shares will be transferable by 
means of a statement included in the title and, in general, by any means permitted by 
law. The transfer of the participation and the address of the new holder will be 
notified by the transferee to the Issuer. 
The Mortgage Shares may be transferred only to institutional or qualified investors 
and specialised professionals. They may not be transferred to the non-specialised 
public. 
The transferor shall not be responsible for the solvency of the Issuer or of the debtor 
of the Participated Mortgage Loan, nor for the mortgage that warrants it being 
sufficient. 
The Issuer shall keep a special book to note the Mortgage Shares issued from each 
Participated Mortgage Loan, as well as any transfers of the same that may be notified 
to it. The provisions on registered titles of Article 53 of the aforementioned Royal 
Decree shall apply to the Mortgage Shares. Any changes of domicile notified to the 
Issuer by the Mortgage Share holders shall be registered by the Issuer in the book. 
In this book, the Issuer shall also record the following data:   
a) 
Date of execution and maturity of the Participated Mortgage Loan, its initial 
amount and liquidation terms.   
b) 
Registration data of the mortgage. 
f) 
Representation of the Mortgage Shares and receiver entities or entities in 
charge of the maintenance of their accounting record in the event of book 
entry 
 
 
111 


 
The Mortgage Shares shall be represented by means of a multiple title issued by the 
Issuer that will contain the minimum mentions that are provided in Article 64 of Royal 
Decree 685/1982, of March 17, modified by Royal Decree 1289/91, of August 2 as 
well as the registration data of the properties that guarantee the Participated 
Mortgage Loans. 
The multiple title representing the Mortgage Shares shall be deposited in the Financial 
Agent, the relationship between the Fund and the Financial Agent being regulated by 
the Financial Services Agreement signed by the Financial Agent and the Managing 
Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund. The deposit shall be constituted for 
the benefit of the Fund so that the Financial Agent will custody the deposited multiple 
title representative of the Mortgage Shares following the instructions of the Managing 
Company. 
g) 
Remuneration system of the Issuer for the management and custody duties 
related to the Participated Mortgage Loans to which paragraph IV.2 below 
refers 
In consideration for the management and custody of the Participated Mortgage Loans, 
the Issuer (or the entity that may replace it in carrying out its duties, if appropriate in 
accordance with the provisions of the Prospectus) shall be entitled to receive, on each 
one of the Payment Dates and while the Management Agreement is in force, a 
subordinated management fee equal to 0.01% per year which shall be accrued and 
paid on a quarterly basis on each Payment Date over the amount of Mortgage Shares 
pending repayment on the referred Payment Date, VAT included. 
The calculation of the fee that will be paid on a given Payment Date, will be made by 
means of the following formula: 
C = B x 0.01% x d/365 
Being: 
C = Fee payable on a given Payment Date.   
B = Amount of Mortgage Shares pending repayment on such Payment Date.   
d = Number of days elapsed during the relevant accrual period (except for the first 
accrual period, where the days elapsed from the Incorporation Date until the first 
Payment Date will be considered). 
Any ordinary expenses incurred by reason of the collection of payments  (including, 
without limitation, telephone or postal expenses) shall be included in the management 
fee. 
The Managing Company will be empowered to agree on a different management fee 
percentage in favour of the replacement entity (even in excess of 0.10% per year), if 
 
 
112 


 
the replacement entity is not a company within Barclays Group, which shall be 
accrued and paid on a quarterly basis on each Payment Date over the amount of 
Mortgage Shares pending repayment on the referred Payment Date, VAT included, if 
the Issuer is removed from its management and custody services, provided that such 
removal is legally possible and appropriate having regards to circumstances which 
might obstruct or make more difficult the proper performance of the above-mentioned 
management duties. 
In the event that Barclays Bank, S.A. is replaced as Manager of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans in any moment during the life of the Fund, the payment of the new 
management fee to the new manager of the Participated Mortgage Loans will rank 3rd 
in the payment priority order established in paragraph V.5.1.B)2 (and 3rd in the 
payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the Fund established in paragraph 
V.6.1), before the payment of the amounts resulting from the settlement of the 
Interest Swap Agreement, if the new manager is not a company within Barclays 
Group. 
In addition, as remuneration or compensation for the financial intermediation 
performed, the Issuer shall be entitled to receive a subordinated, floating amount to 
be settled on a quarterly basis on each Payment Date, which shall accrue on a 
quarterly basis. This amount will be equal to the positive difference, if any, between 
the income and expenses accrued quarterly in accordance with the accounting of the 
Fund, so that the resulting quarterly financial margin is calculated (the "Financial 
Intermediation Margin"). The Financial Intermediation Margin will be paid on each 
Payment Date provided that on such Payment Date there is enough liquidity in 
accordance with paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph 
V.5.2 and the payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the Fund of 
paragraph V.6.1. and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph V.6.2. If there is not 
enough liquidity to pay the Financial Intermediation Margin, the Issuer will lose any 
right to such Financial Intermediation Margin. 
This amount will not have the character of a fee or return due by reason of the 
delivery of a good or the rendering of a service to the Fund, but rather will be 
considered remuneration of the financial intermediation process performed by the 
Issuer by means of the issue of Mortgage Shares grouped in the Fund. 
If the Fund, through its Managing Company, due to a lack of liquidity in accordance 
with the payment priority order set out in paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the exceptional 
rules set out in paragraph V.5.2, does not pay on a Payment Date the entirety of the 
management fee, the unpaid amounts shall be accumulated without penalisation and 
will be paid, if possible, on the following Payment Date, except for the case of 
maintenance of the lack of liquidity. In such a case, the unpaid amounts will be 
postponed to the Payment Date on which the lack of liquidity no longer exists. 
In addition, the Issuer, on each Payment Date, shall be entitled to the reimbursement 
of all expenses of an exceptional nature in which it may have incurred, such as those 
 
 
113 


 
incurred in connection with the enforcement of the mortgage, sale of properties, 
payment of residential properties damage insurance premiums not paid by the 
mortgagors, etc., and prior evidence of them in connection with the management of 
the Participated Mortgage Loans. These expenses will be paid whenever the Fund has 
enough liquidity and in accordance with provisions set forth in paragraphs V.5.1.B)2 
and V.6.1. 
IV.2. 
Succinct and summarised description of the regime and ordinary 
administrative and custody procedures of the Participated Mortgage Loans, 
with special attention given to the procedures established in relation to 
delays and default in payment of principal or interest, early repayments, 
mortgage enforcement and, as the case may be, amendment or 
renegotiation of the loans 
The Issuer, in accordance with article 61.3 of the Royal Decree 685/1982, is under the 
obligation to exercise the custody and management of the Participated Mortgage 
Loans, the relationship between the Issuer and the Fund being regulated by the 
Management Agreement of Participated Mortgage Loans (hereinafter referred to as 
the "Management Agreement") that will be signed by the Issuer (hereinafter and 
with respect to this agreement referred to as "Manager") and the Managing 
Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund. 
The description of the agreements referred to in this Prospectus present fairly the 
most relevant information on the same and does not omit any information which may 
affect the contents of this Prospectus. 
The Manager will continue managing the Participated Mortgage Loans, dedicating the 
same time and attention to them, and managing them with the same level of care and 
diligence as would be exercised in the management of Participated Mortgage Loans 
with respect to which Mortgage Shares have not been issued and, in any case, it will 
exercise an appropriate level of care and diligence in the rendering of the services set 
out in the Management Agreement. 
The Manager renounces, in any case, the privileges and powers that the Law confers 
upon it as manager of the collection of amounts corresponding to the Fund and as 
Manager of the Participated Mortgage Loans and, in particular, those privileges and 
powers provided in the articles 1730 and 1780 of the Civil Code and 276 of Mercantile 
Code. 
The succinct and summarised description of the ordinary procedures for the 
management  and custody (hereinafter, the "Services") of the Participated Mortgage 
Loans regulated by the Management Agreement is the following: 
1. 
Management 
The Manager will maintain the custody and management of the Participated Mortgage 
Loans and will receive, as manager of their collection, on behalf of the Fund, all 
 
 
114 


 
amounts paid by the mortgagors under the Participated Mortgage Loans, immediately 
depositing the amounts corresponding to the Fund in the bank account that the Fund 
maintains in the name of its Manager (the Cash Account). 
2. 
Duration 
The Manager will render the Services until all the Participated Mortgage Loans have 
been fully amortised and all the obligations assumed by the said Manager in 
connection with the Mortgage Shares have been extinguished. 
In the event of insolvency (“concurso”) or liquidation of the Manager, the Managing 
Company shall, if legally possible, designate a new manager of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans who shall accept the obligations set out in the Management 
Agreement. The Rating Agencies shall be duly informed prior to the designation of the 
new manager and shall be furnished with details of the replacement manager and any 
cost associated with the replacement. To avoid damages to the Fund and/or the 
Noteholders, in the event that the Manager is replaced in the management of the 
Participated Mortgage Loans as indicated in this paragraph, the Manager will continue 
performing its duties until the replacement referred to takes place. 
The Manager, once the referred replacement takes place, shall put at the disposal of 
the new manager the documents and computer registrations necessary for the 
performance of the Services. 
In the event that the unsubordinated and unsecured short-term debt of Barclays Bank 
PLC has, at any time, a credit rating lower than A-1 according to the rating scale of 
S&P for short-term risks, or in the case that the holding of Barclays Bank PLC in the 
share capital of the Manager is less than 51% at any time, the Managing Company 
will take whatever action necessary to maintain the then current rating of the Notes. 
The Manager undertakes to assume the measures adopted by the Managing Company 
in the exercise of the faculty established herein. 
3. 
Subcontracting 
The Manager may subcontract, having obtained prior authorisation from the Managing 
Company, any of the Services that it has committed to render, except for those that 
may not be delegated in accordance with the legislation in force, by means of a 
private services agreement. The Manager shall at all times bear the ultimate 
responsibility for the correct management as set out in Law 2/1981, of March 25 on 
the Regulations of the Mortgage Market and in the Royal Decree 685/1982, of March 
17, modified by the Royal Decree 1289/1991, of August 2. The subcontracting will not 
presuppose a revision of the Incorporation Deed or an increase in the price that the 
Fund, through the Managing Company, should pay to the Manager for the rendering 
of the Services. Subcontracting shall be communicated to the Rating Agencies. 
4. 
Responsibility of the Manager 
 
 
115 


 
The Manager commits to act with due diligence in the custody and management of 
the Participated Mortgage Loans and will be accountable to the Fund, through its 
Managing Company, for any harm caused by his negligence. 
5. 
Indemnity of the Manager 
The Manager will indemnify the Fund against any damage, loss or expense incurred 
by reason of the breach by the Manager of its obligations of custody, management 
and information in connection with the Participated Mortgage Loans.   
The Manager does not assume any responsibility by directly or indirectly guaranteeing 
the success of the operation and shall not provide any guarantee or backing, neither 
will it enter into repurchase agreements of the Mortgage Shares, except for those that 
on the Incorporation Date are not in accordance with the conditions and 
characteristics referred to above. 
6. 
Deposit of documents 
The Manager will act as depositary of the deeds of formalisation of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans and all other relevant documents, including, without limitation, 
insurance policies and computer registrations. 
The Manager waives the privileges conferred upon him by law as manager of the 
collections of the Fund and as depositary of the Participated Mortgage Loans and, in 
particular, those contained in articles 1730 and 1780 of the Civil Code (retention as 
pledge of deposited thing) and 276 of the Mercantile Code (a guarantee similar to the 
retention as pledge of deposited thing). 
The Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, will be able to 
examine and the Manager shall provide, the original of the deeds of formalisation of 
the Participated Mortgage Loans, as well as the remaining above mentioned relevant 
documents, deposited with the Manager, whenever the Managing Company deems it 
appropriate, and shall request a copy of any of the above mentioned documents, free 
of charges for a period of no longer than forty eight (48) hours. The Manager shall act 
in the same manner in the case of requests for information by the auditors of the 
Fund. 
7. 
Management of collections 
The Manager, as manager of collections, will receive on behalf of the Managing 
Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, all the amounts paid by the 
mortgagors derived from the Participated Mortgage Loans, both as principal and 
interest, and for any other concept, including the insurance agreements assigned to 
the Managing Company in the name and on behalf of the Fund, owed by virtue of the 
Participated Mortgage Loans, and will deposit the amounts that correspond to the 
Fund, with value of that date, in the Cash Account. 
 
 
116 


 
The Manager will also pay, into the Cash Account and within the same term, any 
amounts received from the mortgagors in early repayment of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans and that are due to the Fund. On the contrary, the Manager will not 
pay the fees received from the mortgagors, as the case may be, as a result of the 
early termination of the Participated Mortgage Loans, as such fees are due to the 
Issuer of the Mortgage Shares. 
In this regard and in accordance with article 1,527 of the Spanish Civil Code, it must 
be noted that the debtor who pays to the former creditor (that is, the Issuer), 
provided that he still does not know that the assignment has been carried out, will be 
free of his obligation. 
8. 
Establishment of Interest Rate 
The Manager will calculate the floating interest rate of the Participated Mortgage 
Loans, in accordance with the provisions set forth in the loan agreements, and will 
communicate to the mortgagors, in the terms set out in these agreements, the 
applicable nominal rate of interest for the following period. 
The Manager will send information regarding the interest rate set, to the debtors 
requesting it and to the Managing Company. 
9. 
Advance of Funds; residential properties damage insurance 
The Manager shall not advance, in any case, any amount that it has not previously 
received from the mortgagors in the form of principal, interest, prepayment or any 
other amount derived from the Participated Mortgage Loans. 
The Manager shall not take or fail to take any action resulting in the cancellation of 
any residential property damage insurance policy or reducing the amount payable in 
any claim thereunder. The Manager shall act diligently and in any event use the rights 
conferred under the insurance policies or the Participated Mortgage Loans deeds in 
order to keep those policies (or any other policy granting equivalent cover) in full 
force and effect in relation to the residential properties mortgaged as security of the 
Participated Mortgage Loans.  
The Manager, except otherwise indicated by the Managing Company, shall be bound 
to anticipate the payment of policy premiums not paid by the mortgagors as soon as it 
becomes aware of this circumstance, without prejudice to its right to be reimbursed 
by the Fund for amounts so paid.  
In the event of a claim, the Manager shall coordinate actions for collecting 
compensations derived from the residential properties damage insurance policies in 
accordance with the terms of the Participated Mortgage Loans deeds and the policies. 
Amounts so received, if any, shall be paid to the Fund. 
10. Forbidden operations; mortgage extension cases 
 
 
117 


 
The Manager shall not i) voluntarily cancel the mortgages corresponding to the 
Mortgage Shares on grounds other than the repayment of the Participated Mortgage 
Loan, ii) waive or enter into a settlement on them, iii) remit the Participated Mortgage 
Loans, wholly or partly, nor extend them, iv) in general, perform any act that may 
decrease the rank, the legal enforceability or the economic value of the mortgage or 
the Participated Mortgage Loans. Notwithstanding this, the Manager may comply with 
the requests of the mortgagors with the same diligence and formality as would be 
exercised with respect to the rest of its loans. 
Nevertheless, in exceptional circumstances and in order to avoid the costs and 
uncertainties inherent in all mortgage enforcement processes and to maintain the 
financial balance of the Fund, and always having regard to the interests of the 
Noteholders, as manager of third parties’ business, the Managing Company shall give 
instructions to the Manager or give it prior authorisation to enter into an agreement 
with a debtor, under the terms and conditions they consider appropriate and pursuant 
to Law 2/1994 on Subrogation and Revision of Mortgage Loans, a novation which 
modifies the Participated Mortgage Loans. In particular, having obtained the prior 
authorisation of the Managing Company (which can only be refused with reasonable 
cause), the Issuer shall agree novations of the Participated Mortgage Loans which 
may imply an increase or a decrease in the remaining term of the relevant 
Participated Mortgage Loan (either for increase or decrease of the repayment term or 
for revision of the repayment method), in all cases subject to the limitations and 
conditions established in the applicable Law and this Prospectus and, in particular, to 
the deadline of the maturity date of the Participated Mortgage Loans (October 29, 
2034), which shall not be exceeded as a result of these novations. 
The Manager will not be entitled under any circumstances (not even at the request of 
the Managing Company) to enter into renegotiations of the interest rate that may 
result in a decrease in the interest rate applicable to a Participated Mortgage Loan. 
The Manager will be authorised to permit subrogations in the position of the 
mortgagor under the Participated Mortgage Loan agreements, exclusively where the 
characteristics of the new mortgagor are similar to those of the former mortgagor and 
those characteristics observe the criteria for granting mortgage loans, the description 
of which will be attached to the Incorporation Deed as an Annex, and provided that 
the expenses derived from that change are fully borne by the mortgagors. The 
Managing Company may fully or partially limit this authority of the Manager or lay 
down conditions therefor. 
Any other renegotiation entered into by the Manager will take place only with the prior 
written consent of the Managing Company. The Manager will request this consent 
from the above mentioned Managing Company as soon as it has knowledge that a 
mortgagor is requesting a renegotiation. 
The Managing Company at any moment during the term of the Management 
Agreement, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, and having given notification to 
 
 
118 


 
the Issuer with reasonable notice and justifiable reasons related to the preservation of 
the financial balance of the Fund, may cancel, suspend or modify the requirements for 
renegotiation by the Manager.   
In the event of any renegotiation of the Mortgage Loan(s), the Manager will 
immediately communicate to the Managing Company the resulting conditions of each 
renegotiation. This communication will be made through the computer file established 
for the update of the conditions of the Participated Mortgage Loans. Both the public 
deeds and the private agreements corresponding to the novation of conditions of the 
Participated Mortgage Loans, will be kept by the Manager, pursuant to paragraph 
IV.2.2. 
In the event of renegotiation of the Participated Mortgage Loans, their maturities, or 
any other condition by the Managing Company in the name and on behalf of the 
Fund, the revision of the conditions will affect the Fund. 
If the Manager had actual knowledge that the value of the property mortgaged in 
security of a Participated Mortgage Loan had decreased by more than the legally 
permitted percentage, he shall immediately inform the Managing Company and, upon 
its request, shall request the borrower to extend the mortgage to other goods in order 
to cover the mandatory relationship between the value of the goods and the secured 
credit, in accordance with articles 26 and 29 of Royal Decree 685/1982. 
If, after the extension has been requested, it is rejected by the mortgagor, he shall 
refund that part of the Participated Mortgage Loan exceeding the amount resulting 
from applying a 80% or that lower percentage determined in the deed of granting of 
the Participated Mortgage Loan to the up-to-date value. The Manager will be under 
the obligation to deposit the amounts he receives from the debtor in favour of the 
Managing Company in this respect in the name and on behalf of the Fund, in the Cash 
Account opened by the Managing Company on behalf of the Fund, described in the 
paragraph following V.3.1. 
If, within two (2) months of this request being made, the mortgagor has not 
performed the extension or returned the part of the corresponding Participated 
Mortgage Loan, it will be understood that that he has opted for the repayment of the 
Participated Mortgage Loan, which will be immediately requested by the Manager. 
Once the amount corresponding to the Participated Mortgage Loan has been received, 
the Manager will immediately deposit, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, the 
relevant part in favour of the Managing Company. 
The debtors may apply for subrogation of a new creditor to the Manager of the 
Participated Mortgage Loans pursuant to Law 2/1994 on Subrogation and Revision of 
Mortgage Loans. Subrogation of a new creditor under the Participated Mortgage Loan 
and the subsequent payment of the amount due will result in the early repayment of 
the Participated Mortgage Loan and of the relevant Mortgage Share. 
 
 
119 


 
Amendments of the Participated Mortgage Loans shall in no event result in an 
alteration of the periodicity of repayment of the principal amount of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans.  
11. Abilities of the holder of the Mortgage Shares in the event of breach of 
their obligations by the mortgagor 
Enforcement action against the mortgagors 
The Manager will use the same diligence and procedures for the reclamation of sums 
of the Participated Mortgage Loans owed and unpaid as with the rest of its loans and, 
especially, it will take the appropriate executive action if its internal processes for 
obtaining satisfaction of the interest of the Fund have not achieved the desired effect 
or if the Managing Company, after analysis of the specific circumstances, considers it 
appropriate, in accordance with the Manager. 
In the event of non-payment by any mortgagor, the Fund, through its Managing 
Company, will have the following abilities pursuant to the provisions set forth in article 
66 of the Royal Decree 685/1982 of March 17, as modified by Royal Decree 1289/91, 
of August 2: 
(a) to compel the Manager to seek the enforcement of the mortgage; 
(b) to take part equally in the rights exercised by the Manager, in its enforcement 
against the debtor, appearing in any enforcement procedure initiated by it, and 
to have a stake in the proceeds of the auction, in proportion to its percentage in 
the enforced loan; 
(c) if the Manager does not begin the procedure within sixty (60) calendar days 
following the notarial diligence of requesting the payment of the debt, the 
Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, will be entitled 
subsidiarily to exercise the enforcement action of the Participated Mortgage Loan 
for the amount corresponding to the percentage of its share, both for principal 
and for interest; and 
(d) in the event that the Manager brings an end to the procedure, the Fund, 
represented by the Managing Company, may subrogate the position of such 
Manager and continue the enforcement procedure without the need for the 
above-mentioned term to have expired. 
In the cases set out in paragraphs (c) and (d), the Managing Company, in the name 
and on behalf of the Fund, may request from the relevant judge the opening of 
proceedings or the continuation of the relevant mortgage enforcement procedure, 
attaching to such formal request the original title of the Mortgage Share, detaching 
the duly attested summons mentioned in paragraph (c) above and the certificate of 
registration and subsistence of the mortgage. 
 
 
120 


 
In the event that the law so requires, and according to Articles 581.2 and 686.2 of 
Law 1/2000, on Civil Prosecution of January 7, the Manager will grant in the 
Incorporation Deed an irrevocable power, as broad and sufficient as required by law 
in favour of the Managing Company, so that it, acting in name and on behalf of the 
Manager, may summon the mortgage debtor of any of the Participated Mortgage 
Loans and demand payment of his debt. 
The Fund, in its capacity as holder of the Mortgage Share and through the Managing 
Company, may also take part in the enforcement procedure with rights equal to those 
of the Manager and may demand, in accordance with Articles 691 et seq. of the Civil 
Prosecution Law, the vesting of the real estate property mortgaged as payment of its 
credit. The Managing Company shall sell the real estate properties assigned as soon 
as it is possible under market conditions. 
Additionally, the Manager must inform the Managing Company about the bad debts, 
early repayments, revisions of interest rates, payment requirements, judicial actions or 
any material circumstance affecting the Participated Mortgage Loans. Likewise, the 
Manager will provide the Managing Company with all documentation required by such 
Manager in connection with such Loans and especially the documentation necessary 
for the filing of judicial actions by the Managing Company, as the case may be. 
Enforcement action against the Issuer 
If the non-payment of the principal amount or interest is not attributable to the non 
payment of the Participated Mortgage Loans’ debtors, the Managing Company, in the 
name and on behalf of the Fund, shall be entitled to an enforcement action against 
the Issuer for the settlement of the maturities of the Mortgage Shares with respect to 
principal and interest. 
Upon the extinguishing of the Participated Mortgage Loans, the Fund, through its 
Managing Company, will reserve the right to take action against the Issuer until it has 
complied in full with its obligations. 
12. 
Liability assumed by the Issuer vis-à-vis the holder of the Mortgage 
Shares 
In accordance with Law 19/1992, the risk of unpaid Mortgage Shares shall be borne 
by the Noteholders. Therefore, the Manager, in its capacity as Issuer, does not 
assume any liability for the non payment of the mortgage debtors, either of principal, 
or of interest or any other amount due by virtue of the Participated Mortgage Loans 
corresponding to the Mortgage Shares. 
 
 
121

indexes of the parameters of early repayment, delays in the payment of 
defaults and bad debt regarding the Mortgage Shares that are grouped in 
the Fund 
The tables shown in the following paragraph V.1.3 refer to one of the possible 
scenarios that, regarding income and payments related to the Fund, may arise during 
the life of the Fund and the issue of the Notes. 
For the preparation of the mentioned charts of the financial service of the Notes and 
of the cash flow of the Fund, the following hypotheses have been used: 
a) 
Participated Mortgage Loans 
(i) 
Number of Participated Mortgage Loans: 4,827  
(ii) Volume of the portfolio on May 16, 2005, from which the loans corresponding to 
the issue of the Mortgage Shares will be extracted: 709,644,270.35 euros. 
(iii) Interest rate: the weighted average interest rate of the Participated Mortgage 
Loans, on May 16, 2005 (when the initial selection of the mortgage loans granted 
by the Issuer took place, on the basis of which the financial formulation of the 
 
 
128 


 
funds has been carried out), was 2.743% per annum and, as a consequence, it has 
been used for the calculation of the income flows of the Fund.   
(iv) CPR: three scenarios at 5%, 10% and 15% yearly. 
(v) Proportion of the Mortgage Shares in arrears: 0%  
(vi) Proportion of the Mortgage Shares in default: 0%. 
b) 
Mortgage Shares 
(i) 
Amount: 700,000,000 euros. 
(ii) Principal: participation of 100%.   
(iii) Interest: participation calculated at the same interest rate applicable to a 
Participated Mortgage Loan. 
c) 
Notes 
(i) 
Volume: 154,000,000 euros of Class A1 Notes, 524,000,000 euros of Class A2 
Notes, 7,000,000 euros of Class B Notes, 7,700,000 euros of Class C Notes and 
7,300,000 euros of Class D Notes. 
(ii) Interest rate: floating interest rate corresponding to the principal balances of each 
of the Classes A1, A2, B, C and D, assuming that the interest rate of each Class 
stays constant at 2.176% for the Class A1 Notes, 2.276% for the Class A2 Notes, 
2.386% the Class B Notes, 2.626% for the Class C Notes and 3.876% for the Class 
D Notes, respectively, for a 3 month Euribor reference interest rate of 2.126%, 
except for the first Interest Accrual Period, in which the sum of the reference 
interest rate resulting from the interpolation and the relevant spread of each Class 
results in a rate of except for the first Interest Accrual Period, in which the sum of 
the reference interest rate resulting from the interpolation and the relevant spread 
of each Class results in a rate of 2.186% for the Class A1 Notes, 2.286 for Class A2 
Notes, 2.396% for Class B Notes, 2.636% for Class C Notes and 3.886% for Class 
D Notes.  
(iii) Exercise by the Issuer of the option of Early Repayment of the Notes of each Class 
when the amount of Mortgage Shares pending repayment is lower than 10% of its 
initial amount. 
 
d) 
Complementary agreements 
(i) 
Cash Account   
The Cash Account will be held with Barclays Bank, S.A., whose obligations are regulated 
in the Financial Services Agreement.    
 
 
129 


 
Interest rate:  monthly average of the EONIA interest rate  (Euro Overnight Interest 
Average) calculated by the European Central Bank and published by REUTERS in its 
page EONIA, corresponding to the previous month, calculated on the balance of the 
account. For the purposes of the calculation of the cash flows of the Fund, it is assumed 
that the balances of the Cash Account accrue an interest equal to 2.070%. As the 
assets are gradually deposited in the Cash Account during the quarter (i.e. they are not 
deposited in the Cash Account during the whole quarter), it is assumed that the income 
of the quarter is equal to 2/3 of the average balance of the Cash Account. 
(ii) Initial Expenses Subordinated Loan Agreement  
Amount: 1,788,250.92 euros, that will be dedicated (i) to financing the incorporation 
expenses of the Fund and the issue of the Notes, (ii) partially, to finance the 
subscription of the Mortgage Shares and (iii) to finance the interest accrued by the 
nominal of the Mortgage Shares between the Incorporation Date and the Disbursement 
Date.    
 
 
 
Repayment: the Initial Expenses Subordinated Loan will be amortised on each Payment 
Date in proportion to the days elapsed on each Interest Accrual Period, taking into 
account a basis of 1,825 days (that is, 5 years with 365 days each), so that it will be 
fully amortised within the term of five (5) years from the incorporation of the Fund. 
Interest rate: equal to the reference interest rate of the Notes (Euribor 3 months or that 
resulting from the interpolation provided in respect of first Interest Accrual Period) 
applicable in the relevant interest period plus a margin of 1.75%. 
(iii) Reserve Fund Subordinated Loan Agreement  
Amount: 6,300,000 euros, which will be allocated to constitute the Reserve Fund. 
Repayment: the Reserve Fund Subordinated Loan will be amortized on each Payment 
Date in proportion to the amortisation of the Reserve Fund, as provided in paragraph 
V.3.3. 
Interest rate: equal to the reference interest rate of the Notes (Euribor 3 months or that 
resulting from the interpolation provided in respect of first Interest Accrual Period) 
applicable in the relevant interest period plus a margin of 1.75%.   
(iv) Reserve Fund
The Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, shall constitute a 
Reserve Fund with the funds received under the Reserve Fund Subordinated Loan 
referred in paragraph V.3.3. 
The amount of the Reserve Fund shall be initially paid into the Cash Account. Its 
allocation, as the case may be, during the life of the Fund, in order to maintain its 
Required Amount, shall be made in accordance with the payment priority order

established in paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the exceptional rules set out in the paragraph 
V.5.2.

Fees and Margin 
(i)

be accrued and paid on a quarterly basis on each Payment Date over the amount 
of Mortgage Shares pending repayment on the referred Payment Date, including 
VAT. 
(ii) Financial Intermediation Margin: variable amount that will be settled on a quarterly 
basis on each Payment Date, and that will accrue quarterly in an amount equal to 
the positive difference, if any, between the income and the expenses of the Fund 
accrued quarterly in accordance with the accounting of the Fund. 
(iii) Ordinary expenses: Euro 27,900 per year.

(i)

V.1.2. 
Analysis and commentary on the impact that the possible variations in the 
hypotheses described in the previous section would have on the financial 
balance of the Fund 
The quality of the Mortgage Shares and the mechanisms guaranteeing the continued 
financial balance of the Fund are such that it is not reasonable to consider percentages 
of advanced amortisation, nor percentages of delay in payment and bad debt so 
extreme that, as a consequence of the mandatory transfer both of the early repayment 
risk and the defaults in the Participated Mortgage Loans, the financial structure of the 
Fund was imbalanced. 
 
 
131 


 
As for the effect that the anticipated reimbursement of the Participated Mortgage Loans 
may have on the Notes, a table of performance of the average life and duration of the 
Notes for different constant rates of early repayment or prepayment (CPR) is included 
in paragraph II.12.b). 
V.1.3. 
Numerical scheme of the flow of income and expenditure of the Fund 
The following numeric scheme makes reference to the collections and payments 
resulting from the application of a “cash basis”, for the greater clarity of the investor, 
although, and in accordance with paragraph V.2, the Fund will make a temporary 
allocation of income and expenses on an “accrual basis”.   
This scheme is based, not only on the assumptions mentioned in the previous 
paragraph V.1.1, but also on the constant maintenance of these assumptions during the 
life of the Fund and, naturally, the affected variables, in particular the interest rates of 
all Classes of Notes, as well as the actual rates of early repayment of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans, are subject to continuing changes.   
Therefore, this numerical scheme serves only as a mere indication.   
All investors interested in receiving information about the situation of the payments of 
the Fund on each specific date, should request the relevant information from those 
institutions authorised to distribute it: Managing Company, AIAF and CNMV.
