V.2. 
Accounting principles used by the Fund 
Income and expenses will be recognised by the Fund following the accrual principle, 
that is, depending on the real cash flow represented by such income and expenses, 
independent of the time at which their collection and payment takes place.   
The fiscal year of the Fund will coincide with the calendar year. However, 
exceptionally, the first fiscal year will begin on the Incorporation Date, and the last 
fiscal year will end on the date on which the extinguishment of the Fund takes place. 
V.3. 
Description of the purpose or target of the financial operations contracted 
by the Managing Company in the name of the Fund in order to diminish the 
risk, increase the frequency of payment, neutralize the difference in 
interest rates coming from the Mortgage Shares, and, in general, to 
transform the financial characteristics of all or part of these securities 
With the purpose of consolidating its financial structure and of procuring the biggest 
possible coverage of the inherent risks of the issue, the Managing Company, in the 
name and on behalf of the Fund, will enter into the agreements set out below, on the 
same date on which the Incorporation Deed is granted.   
The description of the agreements referred to in this Prospectus present fairly the 
most relevant information on the same and does not omit any information which may 
affect the contents of this Prospectus. 
The Managing Company, in order for the operation of the Fund to be performed under 
the terms set out in the Incorporation Deed and according to the regulations in force 
at any time, acting on behalf of the Fund, will be entitled to extend or modify the 
agreements it has entered into on behalf of the Fund, replace any of those rendering 
services to the Fund by virtue of the  agreements and, if necessary, execute additional 
agreements provided always that such actions comply with the legislation in force, 
have been subject to prior authorisation, when necessary, of the CNMV or the 
appropriate administrative body, have been notified to the Rating Agencies, and are 
not prejudicial to the interests of the Noteholders. 
V.3.1. 
Financial Services Agreement 
The Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, and Barclays Bank, 
S.A. (as Financial Agent) will execute a Financial Services Agreement by virtue of 
which the amounts deposited by the Fund through its Managing Company in the Cash 
Account opened with the Financial Agent will accrue an interest rate equal to the 
monthly average of the EONIA rate corresponding to the previous month over the 
balance of the cash account (Euro Overnight Interest Average) calculated by the 
European Central Bank and published by REUTERS in its page EONIA. 
The balances of the Cash Account will be maintained in Euros.   
 


 
In particular, the Financial Services Agreement will determine that the amounts the 
Fund receives in respect of: 
(i) 
principal and interest of the Mortgage Shares;   
(ii) any amounts received in payment of principal or ordinary or arrears interest on 
the Participated Mortgage Loans, also for the auction price or the amounts 
determined by judicial decision or notarial procedure in the enforcement of the 
mortgage guarantees or for the transfer or exploitation of the assets assigned 
when enforcing the mortgage guarantees or as a consequence of the mentioned 
enforcement, in management and interim possession of the properties in 
enforcement processes, as well as all the possible rights or compensation that 
could exist in favour of the Issuer not only including that deriving from the 
damage insurance and accessory rights to the Participated Mortgage Loan 
policies assigned by the Issuer to the Fund, but also those deriving from any 
right attached to the loan; 
(iii) amount of the principal of the executed Participated Mortgage Loans, from the 
date of transfer of the property, acquisition at the auction price or amount 
determined by judicial decision or notarial procedure; 
(iv) the amounts accumulated from the returns obtained by the balances in the Cash 
Account; 
(v) the amounts corresponding to the tax withholdings of the returns on movable 
capital that, as the case may be, in accordance with the legislation in force at any 
time during the life of the Fund, must be effected on each Payment Date from 
the interest of the Notes satisfied by the Fund, until it is required for these 
amounts to be paid to the tax authorities; 
(vi) the amount of the Reserve Fund; and 
(vii) any other amounts representing assets of the Fund at any time,  
will be deposited in the Cash Account initially opened in the books of Barclays Bank, 
S.A. (the Financial Agent), by the Managing Company on behalf of the Fund.  
The balance of the Cash Account will accrue interest at a rate equal to the monthly 
average of the EONIA rate over (Euro Overnight Interest Average) calculated by the 
European Central Bank and published by REUTERS in its page EONIA, corresponding 
to the previous month. This interest will be settled monthly.    
By virtue of the Financial Services Agreement, the Financial Agent will assume 
responsibility for the deposit of the multiple title representing the Mortgage Shares 
subscribed by the Fund. 
 
 
140 


 
In the event that the unsubordinated and unsecured short-term debt of Barclays Bank 
PLC has, at any time, a credit rating lower than A-1, P-1 or F1 (its current ratings 
being A-1+, P-1 and F1+), according to the rating scales of S&P, Moody’s and Fitch 
for short-term risks, respectively, or in the case that the holding of Barclays Bank PLC 
in the share capital of the Financial Agent is less than 51% at any time, the Financial 
Agent, within a period of thirty (30) Business Days following the assignment of this 
lower rating or the decrease in the holding of Barclays Bank PLC in the Financial Agent 
below such percentage: 
(a) shall obtain from a credit entity whose short-term debt has a rating of at least A-
1, P-1 and F1 in accordance with the rating scales of S&P, Moody’s and Fitch for 
short term risks, a joint and several first demand guarantee of the amounts 
deposited in the Cash Account, or 
(b) shall transfer the Cash Account of the Fund to an entity with a non-subordinated 
and unsecured short-term debt of at least A-1, P-1 and F1 ratings (in accordance 
with S&P, Moody’s and Fitch short-term debt rating scales, respectively), 
arranging for the best obtainable return of the balances of the Cash Account, or 
(c) if options a) and b) above are not possible, the Managing Company shall obtain 
from the Financial Agent or a third party collateral security in favour of the Fund 
on financial assets with a credit rating of not less than that of the Spanish State 
Government Debt (“Deuda Pública del Estado Español”), in an amount sufficient 
to guarantee the commitments established in the Financial Services Agreement, 
or 
(d) if none of the above-mentioned measures may be achieved, the Managing 
Company will replace the Financial Agent with another credit entity whose short-
term debt has a rating of at least A-1, P-1 and F1, according to the mentioned 
scales, obtaining the best obtainable return of the balances of the Cash Account. 
In event (b) above, the Managing Company will subsequently re-transfer the balance 
of the Cash Account back to the Financial Agent, provided that the non-subordinated 
and unsecured short-term debt of Barclays Bank PLC is assigned the aforementioned 
A-1, P-1 and F1 ratings and the stake held by Barclays Bank PLC in the Financial 
Agent is equal or higher than 51%. 
The substitution of the Financial Agent will in no event negatively affect the ratings of 
the Notes. 
Likewise, in the event that the ratings on the on the non-subordinated and unsecured 
short-term debt of Barclays Bank PLC falls to A-1 (in accordance with S&P short-term 
debt rating scale), if the balance of the Cash Account exceeds 20% of the Unpaid 
Principal Balance of the Notes on a given Payment Date, the Managing Company will 
deposit the difference on the Excess Balance Account opened by the Managing 
Company in another credit entity whose short-term debt is assigned a minimum rating 
 
 
141 


 
of A-1+ (in accordance the aforementioned rating scale), agreeing for the best 
obtainable return of such balance. Likewise, if Barclays Bank PLC recovers the A-1 
rating (in accordance with S&P short-term debt rating scale), the Managing Company 
may retransfer to the Cash Account opened in the Financial Agent the balance of the 
Excess Balance Account. 
Similarly, in the event that the non-subordinated and unsecured short-term debt of 
Barclays Bank PLC attains again the A-1+ rating (in accordance with S&P short-term 
debt rating scale), the Managing Company will subsequently transfer to the Cash 
Account opened with the Financial Agent the then balance of the Excess Balance 
Account.  
V.3.2. 
Initial Expenses Subordinated Loan Agreement  
The Managing Company will enter into an “Initial Expenses Subordinated Loan 
Agreement” with Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch, in the name and on behalf of 
the Fund, for an amount of ONE MILLION SEVEN HUNDRED EIGHTY EIGHT 
THOUSAND TWO HUNDRED FIFTY EUROS AND NINETY TWO CENTS 
(1,788,250.92€) that will be dedicated (i) to financing the expenses of incorporation 
of the Fund and the issue of the Notes, (ii) partially, to finance the subscription of the 
Mortgage Shares and (iii) to finance the interest accrued on the nominal of the 
Mortgage Shares between the Incorporation Date and the Disbursement Date. 
The “Initial Expenses Subordinated Loan” will accrue a floating nominal interest 
fixed on a quarterly basis that will be equal to the result of adding (i) the interest rate 
of reference of the Notes (3 month Euribor calculated in accordance with paragraph 
II.10 of the Prospectus or that resulting from the interpolation provided in respect of 
the first Interest Accrual Period) applicable in the relevant period of liquidation of 
interest, and (ii) the final spread of Class D Notes. This interest will be paid only if the 
Fund has sufficient liquidity in accordance with the payment priority order laid down in 
paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph V.5.2 and the 
payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the Fund contained in paragraph 
V.6.1. and the exceptional rules established in paragraph V.6.2. The accrued interest 
that will be paid on a given Payment Date will be calculated taking into account: (i) 
the number of days elapsed in each Interest Accrual Period and (ii) a 360 day year. 
The accrued and unpaid interest on a Payment Date, will accrue arrears interest at the 
same rate as the ordinary rate of the Initial Expenses Subordinated Loan, and will be 
paid whenever the Fund has sufficient liquidity and in accordance with the payment 
priority order set out in paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the exceptional rules set out in 
paragraph V.5.2. and the payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the 
Fund contained in paragraph V.6.1. and the exceptional rules established in paragraph 
V.6.2. 
The Initial Expenses Subordinated Loan will be repaid in instalments payable on each 
of the Payment Dates, in proportion to the days elapsed on each Interest Accrual 
 
 
142 


 
Period, taking into account a basis of 1,825 days (that is, 5 years with 365 days each), 
so that it will be fully amortised within a period of five (5) years from the date of 
incorporation of the Fund, provided that the Fund has enough liquidity in accordance 
with the payment priority order set out in paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the exceptional 
rules set out in paragraph V.5.2. and the payment priority order in the event of 
liquidation of the Fund contained in paragraph V.6.1. and the exceptional rules 
established in paragraph V.6.2.  
In the event that the initial expenses of incorporation of the Fund and issuance of the 
Notes and the interest corresponding to the payment deferral of the subscription 
value of the Mortgage Shares were lower than the amount of the Initial Expenses 
Subordinated Loan Agreement, payment of the principal amount of the Initial 
Expenses Subordinated Loan Agreement not allocated to cover said expenses will be 
made in accordance with the exceptional rules of the payment priority order set out in 
paragraph V.5.2. and the exceptional rules of the payment priority order in the event 
of liquidation of the Fund contained in paragraph V.6.2.  
The Initial Expenses Subordinated Loan, due to its subordinated nature, will be 
subordinated with respect to the claims of other creditors of the Fund in the terms set 
out in paragraphs V.5.1.B)2 and V.6.1 , including, among others, the Noteholders. 
V.3.3. 
Reserve Fund Subordinated Loan Agreement  
The Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, will enter into a 
“Reserve Fund Subordinated Loan Agreement” with Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish 
Branch, for an amount of SIX MILLION, THREE HUNDRED THOUSAND EUROS 
(6,300,000 €) which will be allocated to fund the Reserve Fund. 
The “Reserve Fund Subordinated Loan” will accrue a floating nominal interest 
fixed on a quarterly basis that will be equal to the result of adding (i) the interest rate 
of reference of the Notes (3 month Euribor calculated in accordance with paragraph 
II.10 of the Prospectus or that resulting from the interpolation provided in respect of 
the first Interest Accrual Period) applicable in the corresponding period of settlement 
of interest, and (ii) the final spread of Class D Notes. This interest will be paid only if 
the Fund has enough liquidity in accordance with the payment priority order set out in 
paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph V.5.2. and the 
payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the Fund contained in paragraph 
V.6.1. and the exceptional rules established in paragraph V.6.2. The accrued interest 
to be paid on a given Payment Date will be calculated taking into account: (i) the days 
elapsed in each interest accrual period and (ii) a 360 day year. 
Any unpaid interest on a Payment Date will accrue at the same rate as the ordinary 
rate of the Reserve Fund Subordinated Loan, and will be paid whenever the Fund has 
enough liquidity and in accordance with the payment priority order set out in 
paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph V.5.2. and the 
 
 
143 


 
 
 
payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the Fund contained in paragraph 
V.6.1. and the exceptional rules established in paragraph V.6.2.  
Repayment of the Reserve Fund Subordinated Loan will be made on the Final Maturity 
Date or, as the case may be, on each of the Payment Dates, in an amount equal to 
the difference between the Required Amount of the Reserve Fund in the previous 
Payment Date and the Required Amount of the Reserve Fund in the current Payment 
Date. In any event, the first Payment Date on which, if appropriate, the amortisation 
of the Reserve Fund Subordinated Loan will begin will be October 15, 2008 or the first 
Business Day immediately following, as the case may be. 
The Reserve Fund Subordinated Loan, due to its subordinated nature, will be deferred 
with respect to the claims of the other creditors of the Fund in the terms set out in 
paragraphS V.5.1.B)2 and V.6.1, including, inter alia, the Noteholders, except with 
respect to the Initial Expenses Subordinated Loan.
V.3.4. 
Reserve Fund 
The Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, shall constitute a 
Reserve Fund (hereinafter, the “Reserve Fund”) to be funded by the Reserve Fund 
Subordinated Loan described in paragraph V.3.3 above and for an amount equal to 
the amount of such loan.  
The amount of the Reserve Fund shall be initially paid into the Cash Account. Its 
allocation, as the case may be, during the life of the Fund, in order to maintain its 
Required Amount, shall be made in accordance with the payment priority order 
established in section V.5.1.B)2 and the exceptional rules set out in section V.5.2. 
The purpose of such Reserve Fund is to comply with the payment obligations of the 
Fund arising from the categories 1º to 12º of the payment priority order set out in the 
paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph V.5.2. and the 
payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the Fund set out in the paragraph 
V.6.1 and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph V.6.2. 
The “Required Amount of the Reserve Fund” shall be determined in accordance 
with the following rules:  
¾ During the three (3) years from the Incorporation Date of the Fund, the Required 
Amount of the Reserve Fund will be Euros 6,300,000 (the "Initial Required 
Amount of the Reserve Fund").  
¾ Once the term of three (3) years referred to in the previous paragraph has 
elapsed, the new Required Amount of the Reserve Fund (the "New Required 
Amount of the Reserve Fund") will be equal to the lower of (i) Euros 6,300,000 
and (ii) the greater of the following two quantities: 
(i) 
Euros 5,000,000; or 
 
144 


 
(ii) 1.80% of the Unpaid Principal Balance of all Classes on the Calculation 
Date prior to the beginning of the Interest Accrual Period to which such 
Calculation Date refers. 
In any case, the reduction referred to above shall not be carried out in the event 
that, on a given Payment Date, any one of the following three circumstances 
occur: 
(i) 
the Reserve Fund has been used to pay the accrued interest on any one of 
the Classes of Notes on any Payment Date during the life of the Fund; or 
(ii) on the Payment Date prior to the current Payment Date, the Reserve Fund 
is not allocated in the Required Amount of the Reserve Fund on such 
Payment Date; or 
(iii) on the Calculation Date corresponding to the current Payment Date, the 
Principal Balance of the Mortgage Shares with more than ninety (90) days 
in arrears, is equal to or greater than 1% of the Unpaid Principal Balance 
of the Notes.  
V.3.5. 
Interest Swap Agreement 
The Managing Company, acting in the name and on behalf of the Fund, will enter into 
with Barclays Bank PLC Spanish Branch, an interest swap agreement (“Interest 
Swap Agreement”) under the Contrato Marco de Operaciones Financieras -CMOF- 
drawn up by the Spanish Banking Association (Asociación Española de Banca), the 
main characteristics of which are described below. 
The purpose of the execution of the Interest Swap Agreement is to avoid the basis 
risk of floating rate interest which exists in the Fund between the floating rate interest 
of the Participated Mortgage Loans calculated on the basis of 12 Month Euribor, and 
the floating rate interest on the Notes, calculated on the basis of 3 month Euribor and 
with quarterly accrual and settlement (except for the first Interest Accrual Period). 
The purpose is not to avoid the credit risk, which remains at all times with the Fund.   
The credit risk arising from delays in payments of the Participated Mortgage Loans is 
reduced, firstly by means of the Reserve Fund and, secondly, by virtue of the 
subordinated structure of the Class A1, A2, B, C and D Notes, both in respect of 
payment of interest as well as principal, in accordance with the payment priority order 
of the Fund. 
The swap operates as follows, netting of payments being applicable:  
Party A: The Fund, represented by the Managing Company  
Party B: Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch 
 
 
145 


 
1. 
Settlement Date 
The settlement dates (the “Settlement Dates”) will coincide with the Calculation 
Dates. 
2. 
Settlement Period 
Party A: 
The “Settlement Periods” for Party A will be the period between two consecutive 
Settlement Dates, including the first day and excluding the last day. As an exception, 
the first Settlement Period for Party A will begin on the Incorporation Date (inclusive) 
and will end on the first Calculation Date (not inclusive).  
Party B: 
The Settlement Periods for Party B will be the period between two consecutive 
Settlement Dates, including the first day and excluding the last day. As an exception, 
the first Settlement Period for Party B will begin on the Incorporation Date (inclusive) 
and will end on the first Calculation Date (not inclusive).  
3. 
Amounts to be paid by Party A 
On each Payment Date, Party A shall pay an amount equivalent to the sum of the 
amounts collected in the Cash Account and, as the case may be, in the Excess 
Balance Account, of the Fund as ordinary and arrears interest of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans during the Settlement Period. 
Both (i) Accrued Interest (as defined in paragraph IV.1.(b) of the Prospectus) in the 
initial sale of the Mortgage Shares, and (ii) ordinary and arrears interest accrued, prior 
to their subscription date, on the new Mortgage Shares to be issued by the Issuer for 
the substitution of Mortgage Shares in accordance with the rules provided in the 
Incorporation Deed and in paragraph IV.1.(d) of the the Prospectus, shall not be 
considered as ordinary or arrears interest and are expressly excluded for the purposes 
of calculation of the amounts to be paid by Party A.  
The sum of the amounts to be paid by Party A will be the “Amounts to be Paid by 
Party A”. 
4. Amounts to be paid by Party B 
On each Payment Date, Party B shall pay the amount resulting from the application of 
the following rules: 
1. 
Firstly, each “Individual Notional Balance” must be calculated corresponding 
to each of the Participated Mortgage Loans in relation to which ordinary and 
arrears interest collected by the Fund during the relevant Settlement Period has 
 
 
146 


 
been paid.  For this purpose, (i) the amounts collected by the Fund as ordinary 
and arrears interest on each of the Participated Mortgage Loans, shall each be 
divided by (ii) the reference annual interest rate applied to each of the relevant 
Participated Mortgage Loans, plus a margin of 45 basis points (0.45%). The 
result of such division will be the Individual Notional Balance of each Participated 
Mortgage Loan. 
2. 
Secondly, the Individual Notional Balances shall be added together. The result 
will be the “Notional Balance of the Settlement Period”. 
3. 
Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch shall pay an amount equal to the product of 
the Notional Balance of the Settlement Period, multiplied by the 3 month 
EURIBOR (or the interpolation of the 4 month EURIBOR and the 5 month 
EURIBOR for the first Settlement Period, calculated as provided for the reference 
interest rate of the first Interest Accrual Period) interest rate in force on the 
Interest Rate Fixing Date following the Calculation Date which signals the 
commencement of the relevant Settlement Period, plus 43 basis points (0.43%).  
Such amount will be the “Amount to be Paid by Party B”. 
The Amount to be Paid by Party B will be calculated taking into account : (i) the 
number of days elapsed in each Settlement Period and (ii) a 360 day year. The 3 
month EURIBOR interest rate (and the interpolation for the first Interest Accrual 
Period) will be calculated on those dates and in accordance with those procedures set 
out in paragraph II.10.1 for the calculation of the reference EURIBOR interest rate. 
5. 
Net Amount to be paid 
On each Settlement Date only a single amount to be paid on the following Payment 
Date will accrue, whether to be paid by Party A in favour of Party B, or vice versa 
(hereinafter, the “Net Amount”). 
The Net Amount to be paid by Party A to Party B will be the positive difference, if any, 
between the Amount to be Paid by Party A and the Amount to be Paid by Party B.  
The Net Amount to be paid by Party B to Party A will be the positive difference, if any, 
between the Amount to be Paid by Party B and the Amount to be Paid by Party A.  
In the event that on a given Settlement Date the Amount to be Paid by Party B and 
the Amount to be Paid by Party A were one and the same, there would be no Net 
Amount to be paid by either of the Parties to the other on the following Payment 
Date.  
6.  Additional provisions  
If on a given Payment Date the Fund does not have sufficient funds to pay in full the 
amounts owed to Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch, the unpaid amounts shall 
accumulate and arrears interest shall accrue on them at the same rate as that 
 
 
147 


 
provided in the Initial Expenses and Reserve Fund Subordinated Loans. Such unpaid 
amounts will be paid on the next Payment Date on which the Fund has sufficient 
funds in accordance with the payment priority order established in section V.5.1B)2 
and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph V.5.2.  
If the ratings of the unsubordinated and unsecured short-term debt of Barclays Bank 
PLC were to fall, at any time during the life of the Notes, below A-1, P-1 or F1 (its 
current ratings being A-1+, P-1 and F1+) in accordance with the rating  scales of S&P, 
Moody’s and Fitch for short-term risks, or in the event that the unsubordinated and 
unsecured long-term debt of Barclays Bank PLC were to fall, at any time during the 
life of the Notes, below A2 or A (its current being ratings Aa1 and AA+) in accordance 
with the rating scales of Moody’s and Fitch for long-term risks, Barclays Bank PLC, 
Spanish Branch, within a maximum term of thirty (30) days following the date on 
which such circumstance arose:  
(i) 
shall obtain from a credit entity whose unsubordinated and unsecured short-term 
debt has a minimum ratings of A-1, P-1 and F1 in accordance with the rating 
scales of S&P, Moody’s and Fitch for short-term risks and whose unsubordinated 
and unsecured long-term debt has a minimum ratings of A2 and A in accordance 
with the rating scales of Moody’s and Fitch for long-term risks, an on demand 
guarantee of the obligations of Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch under this 
Agreement; or 
(ii) shall constitute a cash or securities collateral in favour of the Fund securing 
fulfilment of the obligations of Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch for an amount 
that, calculated on the basis of the Swap market value of each single contract, 
allows to maintain the ratings assigned to each Series of Notes as required under 
the then in force Rating Agencies' Swap Criteria; or  
(iii) in the event that none of the above-mentioned measures may be achieved, the 
Managing Company will ensure that a third party whose unsubordinated and 
unsecured short-term debt has a minimum ratings of A-1, P-1 and F1 under the 
scales of S&P, Moody’s and Fitch for short-term risks and whose unsubordinated 
and unsecured long-term debt has a minimum ratings of A2 and A under the 
scales of Moody’s and Fitch for long-term risks, assumes the contractual position 
of Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch under the Interest Swap Agreement, either 
by means of subrogation in the Agreement or by means of the execution of a 
new agreement in substantially identical terms as those provided in this 
Agreement and any related contracts. 
In the event that the ratings of the unsubordinated and unsecured short-term debt of 
Barclays Bank PLC were to fall, at any time during the life of the Notes, below A-2, P-2 
or F2 in accordance with the rating scales of S&P, Moody’s and Fitch for short-term 
risks, or in the event that the rating of the unsubordinated and unsecured long-term 
debt of Barclays Bank PLC were to fall, at any time during the life of the Notes, below 
A3 or BBB+ in accordance with the rating scales of Moody’s and Fitch for long-term 
 
 
148 


 
risks, only the measure referred to in (iii) may be taken, and Barclays Bank PLC, 
Spanish Branch shall constitute the cash collateral referred to in option (ii) within a 
term of ten (10) days from the date on which such circumstance occurred until a third 
party replaces it in its contractual position under the Interest Swap Agreement within 
a term of thirty (30) days from the date on which such circumstance has occurred.  
For these purposes, the “Rating Agencies' Swap Criteria” will be the official 
criteria published by S&P, Moody’s and Fitch, respectively, which are in full force and 
effect at each given time and which provide for the rules for the calculation of the 
collateral referred in paragraph (ii) above. 
In any event, such options may not adversely affect the ratings asigned by S&P, 
Moody’s and Fitch to each of the Class A1, A2, B, C and D Notes. 
The occurrence, as the case may be, of the early termination of the Interest Swap 
Agreement (e.g., in the event of material non-fulfilment by Barclays Bank PLC, 
Spanish Branch of its payment obligations or subsequent external events affecting 
Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch) will not constitute in itself an event of early 
repayment of the Notes and early liquidation of the Fund, except in the case that, 
together with other events and circumstances related to the financial situation of the 
Fund, it would give rise to a substantial or permanent financial imbalance. In the 
event of early termination of the Interest Swap Agreement, payment of the Payment 
Amount which may result in favour of Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch will rank 
14th in the payment priority order established in paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the 
exceptional rules set out in paragraph V.5.2. and thirteenth (13th) place in the 
payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the Fund contained in paragraph 
V.6.1. and the exceptional rules established in paragraph V.6.2. 
The Interest Swap Agreement shall be terminated in the event that prior to the 
beginning of the Subscription Period any of the Rating Agencies do not confirm as 
final the provisional ratings assigned to each of the series, except if the Managing 
Company and the Issuer mutually agree in such event to continue with the 
incorporation of the Fund and the issue of the Mortgage Shares and the Notes, if at 
least one of the Rating Agencies confirms its provisional ratings.  
7.  Relevant characteristics 
(i) 
Payments to Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch are calculated on a “cash basis” 
accounting principle, as the interest paid into the Cash Account and, as the case 
may be, into the Excess Balance Account, within each Settlement Period of the 
swap determines the amount to be paid by the Fund to Barclays Bank PLC, 
Spanish Branch on each Payment Date; and 
(ii) Payments by Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch on each Payment Date are also 
calculated on a “cash basis” accounting principle, as they take as a notional 
 
 
149 


 
 
 
balance the floating amount which Party A has to pay on each Settlement Period, 
which is calculated on a “cash basis” accounting principle. 
(iii) In the event that Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish Branch is replaced as counterparty 
in the Interest Swap Agreement, references to Barclays Bank PLC, Spanish 
Branch in the payment priority order established in paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the 
exceptional rules set out in paragraph V.5.2. and the payment priority order in 
the event of liquidation of the Fund contained in paragraph V.6.1. and the 
exceptional rules established in paragraph V.6.2., shall be understood to be made 
to the new counterparty.
V.4. 
Other agreements   
The description of the agreements referred to in this Prospectus present fairly the 
most relevant information on the same and does not omit any information which may 
affect the contents of this Prospectus. 
V.4.1. 
Management Agreement (Participated Mortgage Loans)   
The Issuer, in accordance with the provisions set forth in the Incorporation Deed and 
in accordance with the Royal Decree 685/1982, of March 17, on the regulation of 
certain aspects of the Mortgage Market, modified by the Royal Decree 1289/1991, of 
August 2, will enter into, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, a Management 
Agreement with the Managing Company by virtue of which it will provide, as agent of 
the Fund, (i) the custody and management of the Participated Mortgage Loans; and 
(ii) will receive, in the collection management, on behalf of the Fund, all amounts 
satisfied by the mortgagors with respect to their Participated Mortgage Loans, and will 
deposit the amounts that correspond to the Fund, according to paragraph IV.2.8, in 
the Cash Account described in paragraph V.3.1. 
In accordance with paragraph IV.1.g), in return for the services to be rendered by the 
management of the Participated Mortgage Loans, the Issuer will be entitled to receive 
on each of the Payment Dates and while the Management Agreement is in force, an 
annual subordinated management fee of 0.01% which shall be accrued and paid on a 
quarterly basis on each Payment Date over the amount of Mortgage Shares pending 
repayment on the referred Payment Date, VAT included, whenever the Fund has 
sufficient liquidity and once the payment obligations have been complied with, 
according to the payment priority order of the Fund described in paragraph V.5.1.B)2 
and the exceptional rules set out in the paragraph V.5.2. and the payment priority 
order in the event of liquidation of the Fund contained in paragraph V.6.1. and the 
exceptional rules established in paragraph V.6.2. 
The Managing Company will be empowered to agree on a different management fee 
percentage in favour of the replacement entity (even in excess of 0.10% per year), if 
the replacement entity is not a company within Barclays Group, which shall be 
accrued and paid on a quarterly basis on each Payment Date over the amount of 
Mortgage Shares pending repayment on the referred Payment Date, VAT included, if 
 
150 


 
the Issuer is removed from its management and custody services, provided that such 
removal is legally possible and appropriate having regards to circumstances which 
might obstruct or make more difficult the proper performance of the above-mentioned 
management duties. 
In the event that Barclays Bank, S.A. is replaced as Manager of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans in any moment during the life of the Fund, the payment of the new 
management fee to the new manager of the Participated Mortgage Loans will rank 3rd 
in the payment priority order established in paragraph V.5.1.B)2 (and 3rd in the 
payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the Fund established in paragraph 
V.6.1.), before the payment of the amounts resulting from the settlement of the 
Interest Swap Agreement, if the new manager is not a company within Barclays 
Group. 
In addition, as remuneration or compensation for the financial intermediation 
performed, the Issuer shall be entitled to receive a subordinated, floating amount to 
be settled on a quarterly basis on each Payment Date, which shall accrue on a 
quarterly basis. This amount will be equal to the positive difference, if any, between 
the income and expenses accrued quarterly in accordance with the accounting of the 
Fund, so that the resulting quarterly financial margin is calculated (Financial 
Intermediation Margin). The Financial Intermediation Margin will be paid on each 
Payment Date provided that on such Payment Date there is enough liquidity in 
accordance with paragraph V.5.1.B)2 and the exceptional rules set out in paragraph 
V.5.2. and the payment priority order in the event of liquidation of the Fund contained 
in paragraph V.6.1. and the exceptional rules established in paragraph V.6.2. If there 
is not enough liquidity to pay the Financial Intermediation Margin, the Issuer will lose 
any right to such Financial Intermediation Margin. 
V.4.2. 
Underwriting Agreement 
The Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, will execute an 
Underwriting Agreement for the issue of the Notes subject to English law with the 
Underwriting Entities, whereby the Underwriting Entities will distribute the Notes in 
the amounts set out for each one in paragraph II. 19. 1, and once the Subscription 
Period has expired, they will subscribe on their own behalf the amount of Notes 
pending subscription, by virtue of their underwriting obligation. 
The Underwriting Entities assume the obligations provided in the Underwriting 
Agreement, which are basically as follows: 1) undertaking to subscribe for the Notes 
which have not been subscribed once the Subscription Period is closed, up to the 
amounts set out for each of them; 2) payment into the bank account opened by the 
Financial Agent (Barclays Bank, S.A.) at the Bank of Spain, of the underwriting 
commitment by each Underwriting Entity, for same-day value, before 11:00 hours 
a.m. (Madrid time) on the Disbursement Date, after deduction of the agreed 
underwriting fee; and 3) delivery of a subscription supporting document to 
subscribers.  
 
 
151 


 
The Underwriting Entities of the issue of the Notes will receive an underwriting fee of 
0.10% over the total nominal amount of Notes underwritten. The payment of this fee 
will be charged to the Fund on the Disbursement Date by means of the deduction of 
deduction of the payable fee from the amount effectively underwritten that the 
relevant Underwriting Entity will pay to the Financial Agent in the account opened with 
the Bank of Spain in the name of Barclays Bank, S.A., as provided in the Underwriting 
Agreement. 
 
The Entidad Directora will receive an arrangement fee of 0.01% of the nominal 
amount of the issue of the Notes. The Entidad Directora will be entitled to the 
payment of the arrangement fee by the Fund on the Disbursement Date, by means of 
its deduction from the amounts received from the Underwriting Entities which the 
Financial Agent shall pay to the Fund in the Cash Account. 
 
The underwriting commitment contained herein is provisional and subject to the 
Managing Company, the Entidad Directora and the Underwriting Entities reaching an 
agreement on the final spreads applicable to all Classes of Notes before the 
commencement of the Subscription Period. If an agreement is not reached (or in the 
event that the Underwriting Entities invoke any of the conditions for termination 
established below), the Underwriting Entities which do not accept the final spreads (or 
who have invoked any of the conditions for termination established below) shall be 
free from their commitments and the Managing Company will be entitled to determine 
the final spreads on its own. In this case, Barclays Bank, S.A. undertakes to fully 
assume the underwriting commitments of those Underwriting Entities which do not 
accept the final spreads or who have invoked any of the conditions for termination 
established below and will be entitled to receive in turn an underwriting fee of 0.10% 
over the total nominal amount of Notes underwritten by it. In this case, the Managing 
Company shall communicate to the CNMV that Barclays Bank, S.A. will finally act as 
Underwriting Entity by virtue of this underwriting commitment. 
The said underwriting commitment will be included in a second underwriting and 
arrangement agreement, subject to Spanish law, and subject to the conditions (only 
with regard to the underwriting commitment of Barclays Bank, S.A. but not to the 
same acting as Entidad Directora) referred to in paragraph II.19.1. This underwriting 
agreement will be entered into by the Managing Company, in the name and on behalf 
of the Fund, with Barclays Bank, S.A. The terms and conditions of this underwriting 
agreement subject to conditions precedent will be substantially the same than the 
Underwriting Agreement, except for those operating terms which need to be altered 
by reason of the Financial Agent acting as Underwriting Entity.  
V.4.3. 
Financial Services Agreement (Agency of Payments of the Notes) 
The Managing Company, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, will enter into a 
Financial Services Agreement with Barclays Bank, S.A. (see paragraph V.3.1), to 
perform financial servicing services in connection with the issue of the Notes.   
 
 
152 


 
The obligations contained in the Financial Services Agreement with regard to 
payments are basically as follows:   
(i) 
on each Payment Date, to pay interest and to repay principal of the Notes, once 
deduction has been made for the tax withholding for movable capital gains that 
may have to be made in accordance with the applicable tax legislation, as well as 
to pay the remaining amounts that have to be paid by the Fund in accordance 
with the Prospectus; and   
(ii) on each Interest Rate Fixing Date, to communicate to the Managing Company 
the Euribor reference interest rate that will serve as the base for the calculation 
of the applicable nominal rate of interest to each of the Classes of the Notes. 
In return for the services rendered in accordance with the Financial Services 
Agreement, the Financial Agent will be entitled to receive from the Fund for the 
periods expired on each Payment Dates, a fee of 0.002% per annum of the Unpaid 
Principal Balance of the Notes on the last Payment Date. 
In the event that at any time during the life of the Fund the ratings of Barclays Bank 
PLC or its stake in Barclays Bank, S.A. fall below the thresholds indicated in paragraph 
II.4.1 above, Barclays Bank, S.A. will be replaced by another credit entity whose 
short-term debt has a rating of at least A-1 in accordance with the rating scale of S&P 
for short-term risks, P-1 in accordance with the rating scale of Moody’s for short-term 
risks and F1 in accordance with the rating scale of Fitch for short-term risks (in which 
case, the Managing Company will transfer to this entity the Cash Account and will 
arrange for the best obtainable return of its balances), unless the Financial Agent, 
within thirty (30) Business Days from the assignment of this lower rating or from the 
reduction of Barclays Bank PLC’s holding in the Financial Agent below the above 
mentioned percentage, (i) finds a credit entity with the mentioned minimum ratings, 
able to provide a first demand guarantee which guarantee for the Fund, at the 
Managing Company’s request, the amounts deposited in the Cash Account, or (ii) 
transfer the Cash Account of the Fund to an entity with a non-subordinated and 
unsecured short-term debt of at least A-1, P-1 and F1 ratings (in accordance with 
S&P, Moody’s and Fitch short-term debt rating scales, respectively), arranging for the 
best obtainable return of the balances of the Cash Account, or (iii) if options a) and b) 
above are not possible, the Managing Company obtains from the Financial Agent or a 
third party collateral security in favour of the Fund on financial assets with a credit 
rating of not less than that of the Spanish State Government Debt (“Deuda Pública del 
Estado Español”) in an amount sufficient to guarantee the commitments established in 
the Financial Services Agreement. In event (ii) above, the Managing Company will 
subsequently re-transfer the balances of the Cash Account back to the Financial 
Agent, provided that the non-subordinated and unsecured short-term debt of Barclays 
Bank PLC is assigned the aforementioned A-1, P-1 and F1 ratings and the stake held 
by Barclays Bank PLC in the Financial Agent is equal or higher than 51%. The 
substitution of the Financial Agent will in no event negatively affect the ratings of the 
Notes. Likewise, in the event that the ratings on the on the non-subordinated and 
 
 
153 


 
unsecured short-term debt of Barclays Bank PLC falls to A-1 (in accordance with S&P 
short-term debt rating scale), if the balance of the Cash Account exceeds 20% of the 
Unpaid Principal Balance of the Notes on a given Payment Date, the Managing 
Company will deposit the difference on the Excess Balance Account opened by the 
Managing Company in another credit entity whose short-term debt is assigned a 
minimum rating of A-1+ (in accordance the aforementioned rating scale), agreeing for 
the best obtainable return of such balance. Similarly, in the event that the non-
subordinated and unsecured short-term debt of Barclays Bank PLC attains again the 
A-1+ rating (in accordance with S&P short-term debt rating scale), the Managing 
Company will subsequently transfer to the Cash Account opened with the Financial 
Agent the then balance of the Excess Balance Account.  
In the event that the Issuer was substituted in its duties of Financial Agent, provided 
that it is legally possible and adequate having regard to the circumstances which may 
impede or make the correct performance of such functions difficult, the Managing 
Company will be entitled to increase the fee percentage in favour of the new financial 
agent up to a maximum of 0.10% per year of the Unpaid Principal Balance of the 
Notes on the prior Payment Date, if the new financial agent is not a company within 
Barclays Group. 
V.5. 
Rules of priority set forth in the payments of the Fund 
V.5.1. 
Ordinary rules of payment priority of the Fund 
Origin and application of the funds  
A) On the Disbursement Date of the Notes 
The origin and application of the amounts available to the Fund on the Disbursement 
Date of the issue of Notes will be as follows: 
1. Origin: the Fund will be provided with the funds derived for the following concepts: 
(a) Disbursement of the issue of the Notes 
(b) Amount drawn under the Initial Expenses Subordinated Loan 
(c) Amount drawn under the Reserve Fund Subordinated Loan 
2. Application: the Fund, in turn, will apply the funds mentioned above to the 
following expenses: 
(a) Purchase of the Mortgage Shares, both their nominal amount and the interest 
corresponding to the payment deferral of such nominal amount from the 
Incorporation Date to the Disbursement Date 
(b) Payment of the expenses of incorporation of the Fund and issue of the Notes

of the Notes 
1. 
Origin: the available funds (the “Available Funds”) in order to comply with 
the payment or withholding obligations listed below in subparagraph 2 will be the 
following: 
a) 
the amounts received from the repayment of principal of the Mortgage 
Shares, which may have been deposited in the Cash Account and, as the case may 
be, in the Excess Balance Account, in accordance with paragraph V.3.1; 
b) the ordinary and arrears interest collected from the Mortgage Shares which may 
have been deposited in the Cash Account and, as the case may be, in the Excess 
Balance Account, by the Issuer on each collection date, in accordance with the 
paragraph V.3.1; 
c) the amount of the Reserve Fund; 
d) the amounts that, as the case may be, may accrue in favour of the Fund on each 
Settlement Date (which coincide with the Calculation Date) and will be collected in the 
next Payment Date under the Interest Swap Agreement; 
e) the reinvestment of the amounts deposited in the Cash Account and, as the case 
may be, in the Excess Balance Account; 
f) 
any other amounts that the Fund may receive including those which may result 
from the transfer of the real estate assigned to it, or its exploitation.

Class A1 Notes and payment of Principal Due for Repayment of the Class A2 Notes 
which, in turn, will be in 5th and 6th place in the payment priority order, respectively. 
Such deferral of payment of interest on Class B Notes will be irreversible. Accordingly, 
upon occurrence of the same on a Payment Date, interest on Class B Notes will be 
deferred on each subsequent Payment Date until full repayment of Class B Notes, 
even if the aforementioned ratio falls below 150%.

Balance of the Class C and D Notes on such Payment Date, then the payment of 
accrued interest of the Class C Notes will be in 9th place in the payment priority order, 
after the payment of the Principal Due for Repayment of the Class B Notes which, in 
turn, will be in 8th place in the payment priority order. and the order of the preceding 
items would be, if appropriate, subsequently altered as provided herein. Such deferral 
of payment of interest on Class C Notes will be irreversible. Accordingly, upon 
occurrence of the same on a Payment Date, interest on Class C Notes will be deferred 
on each subsequent Payment Date until full repayment of Class C Notes, even if the 
aforementioned ratio falls below 150%. 
7th  
Payment of accrued interest on the Class D Notes. In the event that on any 
given Payment Date the Principal Deficiency exceeds 200% of the Unpaid Principal 
Balance of the Class D Notes on such Payment Date, then the payment of accrued 
interest of the Class D Notes will be in 11th place in the payment priority order, after 
the payment of the Principal Due for Repayment of the Class C Notes which, in turn, 
will be in 10th place in the payment priority order, and the order of the preceding 
items would be, if appropriate, subsequently altered as provided herein. Such deferral 
of payment of interest on Class D Notes will be irreversible. Accordingly, upon 
occurrence of the same on a Payment Date, interest on Class D Notes will be deferred 
on each subsequent Payment Date until full repayment of Class D Notes, even if the 
aforementioned ratio falls below 200%.

157 


 
Available Principal Funds for Repayment will be allocated for repayment of principal of 
all Classes in accordance with the following rules: 
1st Available Principal Funds for Repayment shall be fully allocated for repayment of 
Class A1 Notes until the Payment Date on which Class A1 Notes have been fully 
repaid. 
2nd Once Class A1 Notes have been fully repaid and until the first Payment Date 
(included) on which the Unpaid Principal Balance of Class B, Class C and Class D 
Notes represents at least 6.3% of the Unpaid Principal Balance of all Classes of Notes, 
the Available Principal Funds for Repayment shall be solely allocated for repayment of 
Class A2 Notes.  
3rd After the Payment Date on which the ratio between the Unpaid Principal Balance 
of Class B, Class C and Class D Notes and the Unpaid Principal Balance of all Classes 
of Notes, is equal or greater than 6.3%, the Available Principal Funds for Repayment 
shall be allocated for repayment of Class A2, B, C and D Notes, pro rata among them, 
in such a way that the ratio remains at 6.3% or the nearest higher percentage. 
This notwithstanding, pro rata repayment of Class A2, B, C and D Notes shall be 
interrupted and the Available Principal Funds for Repayment shall be allocated for 
repayment of the Classes on a sequential basis in accordance with their priority order 
on any Payment Date on which any of the following circumstances occurs: 
a) 
The Principal Balance of the Mortgage Shares with a delay in payment of 
overdue amounts greater than ninety (90) days is higher than 2% of the 
Principal Balance of the Mortgage Shares on the Calculation Date corresponding 
to the current Payment Date. 
b) 
The amount of the Reserve Fund is lower than its Required Amount. 
Once the circumstances producing the interruption in the pro rata repayment of 
Classes A2, B, C and D have disappeared, the referred pro rata repayment will be 
carried out again.  
4th After the first Payment Date on which the amount of Mortgage Shares pending 
repayment is lower than 10% of their initial amount, pro rata repayment of Classes 
A2, B, C and D Notes shall be interrupted and the Available Principal Funds for 
Repayment shall be allocated for repayment of the Classes on a sequential basis in 
accordance with their priority order until their repayment is completed. 
V.5.2. 
Exceptional Rules of payment priority with charge to the Fund 
In the event that Barclays Bank, S.A. is replaced as Manager of the Participated 
Mortgage Loans in any moment during the life of the Fund, the payment of the 
management fee to the new manager of the Participated Mortgage Loans (which may 
be higher if the new manager is not a company within Barclays Group), will rank 3rd in 
 
 
158 


 
the payment priority order, before the payment of the amounts resulting from each 
settlement of the Interest Swap Agreement, if the new manager is not a company 
within Barclays Group.  
In such case, (i) the references made in this Prospectus to the items between 3rd and 
18th of the payment priority order, will be understood each as made to the items 
between 4th and 19th, respectively, (ii) the item relating to the payment to the Issuer 
of the fee for the management of the Participated Mortgage Loans in accordance with 
the Management Agreement (referred to before as ranked 19th) will be deleted, and 
(iii) the references made in this Prospectus to the items 1st, 2nd and 20th of the 
payment priority order shall be unaffected. 
Likewise, in the event that the initial expenses of incorporation of the Fund and 
issuance of the Notes and the interest corresponding to the payment deferral of the 
subscription value of the Mortgage Shares were lower than the amount of the Initial 
Expenses Subordinated Loan Agreement, payment of the principal amount of the 
Initial Expenses Subordinated Loan Agreement not allocated to cover said expenses 
will be in 18th place in the payment priority order. In that event, references made in 
this Prospectus to the items 18th to 20th of the payment priority order shall be 
understood to have been made to items 19th to 21th , respectively.

In accordance with Law 19/1992, of July 7, on the Regime applicable to Companies and Real 
Estate Investment Funds and on Mortgage Securitisation Funds, Mortgage Securitisation Funds 
do not have legal capacity, Management Companies of Securitisation Funds are responsible for 
their incorporation, management and legal representation, as well as the representation and 
defence of the interests of the holders of the issued securities at the expense of the Funds that 
they manage. 
By virtue of the foregoing, this Chapter provides details concerning AHORRO Y TITULIZACIÓN, 
S.G.F.T. S.A., as Managing Company that constitutes, manages and represents AyT Génova 
Hipotecario VI, FTH.

Valores (CNMV) 
AHORRO Y TITULIZACIÓN, SOCIEDAD GESTORA DE FONDOS DE TITULIZACIÓN, S.A. 
was incorporated through a public deed executed on November 16, 1993, before Mr. 
Francisco Javier Die Lamana, Notary Public of Madrid, under number 2609, of his 
public records. Prior authorisation of the Ministry of Economy and Finance was 
granted on July 16, 1993. It was registered on  the Mercantile Register of Madrid 
(Volume 7240, Folio 191, Book 0, Section 8, Sheet number M-117365, entry one). It is 
registered with the Special CNMV Register under number 5.

occurrence of any of the circumstances which legal or statutory provisions, as the 
case may be, may establish as reasons for dissolution.

VII.1. More recent and significant trends in the mortgage market in general and, in 
particular, in the mortgage loans market, in connection with their legal 
framework including the evolution of interest rates, early repayment 
indexes and delays in payment 
The Spanish mortgage market has experienced an important transformation in recent 
years, both in relation to its legal framework and the predominant interest that the 
credit entities have developed therein. 
The most recent regulations have purported to provide mortgagors with greater powers 
of negotiation of loan conditions, as well as to reduce certain costs related to their re-
negotiation. In this sense, besides Law 2/94, of March 30, on Subrogation and Revision 
of Mortgage Loans (which regulates the possibilities of substitution and renegotiation of 
the economic conditions of the loans with a reduction of costs, both fiscal and tariff, as 
well as a reduction of early repayment fees for loans with a floating interest rate), two 
measures were adopted with the aim of reducing the costs of subrogation operations 
and modifying novation of mortgage loans: on the one hand, the agreement entered 
into by the Ministry of Economy with banks and saving banks, reducing fees; and on 
the other hand, the approval of Royal Decree 2616/1996, of December 20, and Royal 
Decree-Law 2/2003, of April 25, by means of which, among other measures, the notary 
and registry tariffs were modified for operations of subrogation and novation of 
mortgage loans subject to the said Law 2/94. 
Additionally, the significant reduction in interest rates which has taken place during the 
last few years, together with the increase in the competitiveness of the credit entities in 
this sector of the financing industry, with the aim of gaining the trust of their clients, 
has lead to a considerable increase in the rates of advance repayment of mortgage 
loans which have interest rates above the predominant rate in the mortgage market at 
the time, due to the lack of offers to renegotiate conditions on the part of lenders. 
Nevertheless, it should be kept in mind that the early repayment of the mortgage loans 
will take place irrespective of Law 2/1994, since the early repayment of loans depends 
not only on the favourable provisions of the law, but also on more decisive factors, 
fundamentally, its age and the higher rate of interest in relation others being offered at 
that time. 
 
 
166 


 
VII.2. Implications that could be derived from the trends commented in section 
VII.1 (index of early repayments, index of bad debt, etc.) 
All the mortgage loans participated by the Mortgage Shares subscribed by the Fund, 
are subject to a floating interest rate, which may be varied periodically in accordance 
with the variations in the market interest rates; therefore, a high rate of early 
repayment of Participated Mortgage Loans is not envisaged.
